import { mutation, internalMutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";

// Public seeder - call once to populate demo data
export const seedDemo = mutation({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx): Promise<{ seeded: boolean; message: string }> => {
    // Check if already seeded
    const existing = await ctx.db.query("categories").first();
    if (existing) return { seeded: false, message: "Already seeded" };

    // Seed categories
    const catIds: Record<string, string> = {};
    const cats = [
      { name: "Templates", slug: "templates", icon: "Layout", color: "#3b82f6" },
      { name: "Plugins", slug: "plugins", icon: "Plug", color: "#8b5cf6" },
      { name: "AI Tools", slug: "ai-tools", icon: "Sparkles", color: "#ec4899" },
      { name: "Games", slug: "games", icon: "Gamepad2", color: "#10b981" },
      { name: "Gift Cards", slug: "gift-cards", icon: "Gift", color: "#f59e0b" },
      { name: "IPTV", slug: "iptv", icon: "Tv", color: "#06b6d4" },
    ];
    for (const c of cats) {
      const id = await ctx.db.insert("categories", { ...c, description: null });
      catIds[c.slug] = id;
    }

    // Seed vendors
    const vendorIds: string[] = [];
    const vendorData = [
      { storeName: "PixelCraft Studio", slug: "pixelcraft", verified: true, totalSales: 1200, totalRevenue: 48000, rating: 4.8 },
      { storeName: "NovaLabs", slug: "novalabs", verified: true, totalSales: 890, totalRevenue: 35600, rating: 4.6 },
      { storeName: "Lumen Games", slug: "lumengames", verified: true, totalSales: 430, totalRevenue: 12900, rating: 4.7 },
      { storeName: "SecureStack", slug: "securestack", verified: false, totalSales: 210, totalRevenue: 8400, rating: 4.5 },
      { storeName: "PayBridge Labs", slug: "paybridgelabs", verified: true, totalSales: 660, totalRevenue: 26400, rating: 4.4 },
    ];
    for (const v of vendorData) {
      const id = await ctx.db.insert("vendors", { ...v, commissionRate: 15, logo: null, description: null });
      vendorIds.push(id);
    }

    // Seed products
    const productData = [
      { title: "Crypto Dashboard Kit", type: "TEMPLATE", price: 49, salesCount: 340, categoryId: catIds["templates"], vendorId: vendorIds[0] },
      { title: "NovaScript AI Writer", type: "AI_TOOL", price: 39, salesCount: 520, categoryId: catIds["ai-tools"], vendorId: vendorIds[1] },
      { title: "Neon Drift Racer", type: "GAME", price: 19, salesCount: 180, categoryId: catIds["games"], vendorId: vendorIds[2] },
      { title: "SecureAuth Pro", type: "PLUGIN", price: 59, salesCount: 210, categoryId: catIds["plugins"], vendorId: vendorIds[3] },
      { title: "Stripe Connect Kit", type: "PLUGIN", price: 89, salesCount: 290, categoryId: catIds["plugins"], vendorId: vendorIds[4] },
      { title: "ResumeBoost AI Coach", type: "AI_TOOL", price: 29, salesCount: 410, categoryId: catIds["ai-tools"], vendorId: vendorIds[1] },
      { title: "Neon UI Component Kit", type: "TEMPLATE", price: 69, salesCount: 155, categoryId: catIds["templates"], vendorId: vendorIds[0] },
      { title: "Steam $50 Gift Card", type: "GIFT_CARD", price: 50, salesCount: 800, categoryId: catIds["gift-cards"], vendorId: vendorIds[0] },
      { title: "IPTV Premium 6 Months", type: "IPTV", price: 25, salesCount: 650, categoryId: catIds["iptv"], vendorId: vendorIds[4] },
      { title: "SheetFlow Automation", type: "PLUGIN", price: 44, salesCount: 230, categoryId: catIds["plugins"], vendorId: vendorIds[3] },
    ];
    const productIds: string[] = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < productData.length; i++) {
      const p = productData[i];
      const id = await ctx.db.insert("products", {
        title: p.title,
        slug: p.title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-"),
        shortDescription: `Premium ${p.type.toLowerCase()} for professionals`,
        description: `Fully featured ${p.title} with extensive documentation and support.`,
        type: p.type,
        status: "ACTIVE",
        price: p.price,
        discountPrice: i % 3 === 0 ? Math.round(p.price * 0.8) : undefined,
        currency: "USD",
        sku: `PB-${1000 + i}`,
        stock: null,
        coverType: "gradient",
        coverColors: [["#3b82f6", "#8b5cf6"], ["#ec4899", "#f59e0b"], ["#10b981", "#06b6d4"]][i % 3],
        tags: [p.type.toLowerCase(), "premium"],
        licenseType: "SINGLE",
        featured: i < 4,
        rating: 4.3 + (i % 5) * 0.1,
        reviewCount: 20 + i * 8,
        salesCount: p.salesCount,
        vendorId: p.vendorId,
        categoryId: p.categoryId,
      });
      productIds.push(id);
    }

    // Seed orders
    const statuses = ["COMPLETED", "PAID", "PENDING", "REFUNDED", "CANCELLED"];
    const customers = [
      { name: "Alex Johnson", email: "alex@example.com" },
      { name: "Maria Garcia", email: "maria@example.com" },
      { name: "James Lee", email: "james@example.com" },
      { name: "Sara Smith", email: "sara@example.com" },
      { name: "Tom Brown", email: "tom@example.com" },
    ];
    for (let i = 0; i < 25; i++) {
      const customer = customers[i % customers.length];
      const product = productData[i % productData.length];
      await ctx.db.insert("orders", {
        orderNumber: `PB-${1000 + i}`,
        customerName: customer.name,
        customerEmail: customer.email,
        status: statuses[i % statuses.length],
        paymentStatus: i % 5 === 3 ? "REFUNDED" : "PAID",
        subtotal: product.price,
        discount: 0,
        total: product.price,
        provider: ["STRIPE", "PAYPAL", "JAZZCASH"][i % 3],
        items: [{ productId: productIds[i % productIds.length], title: product.title, price: product.price, licenseKey: `LIC-${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10).toUpperCase()}` }],
      });
    }

    // Seed notifications
    const notifs = [
      { type: "ORDER", title: "New order received", message: "Alex Johnson purchased Crypto Dashboard Kit for $49" },
      { type: "VENDOR", title: "Vendor verified", message: "SecureStack has been verified" },
      { type: "REVIEW", title: "New review flagged", message: "Suspicious review detected on SheetFlow Automation" },
      { type: "SYSTEM", title: "Revenue milestone", message: "Congratulations! You hit $50,000 in total revenue" },
      { type: "ORDER", title: "Refund processed", message: "Order #PB-1019 has been refunded — $44" },
    ];
    for (const n of notifs) {
      await ctx.db.insert("notifications", { ...n, read: false });
    }

    // Seed settings
    const settingsData = [
      { key: "site_name", value: "PlayBeat Digital", category: "general" },
      { key: "currency", value: "USD", category: "general" },
      { key: "commission_rate", value: "15", category: "commerce" },
      { key: "maintenance_mode", value: "false", category: "system" },
      { key: "stripe_active", value: "true", category: "payments" },
      { key: "paypal_active", value: "true", category: "payments" },
      { key: "jazzcash_active", value: "true", category: "payments" },
      { key: "lemon_squeezy_active", value: "true", category: "payments" },
    ];
    for (const s of settingsData) {
      await ctx.db.insert("settings", s);
    }

    // Seed coupons
    const couponData = [
      { code: "WELCOME20", type: "PERCENTAGE", value: 20, minPurchase: 0, active: true, usageLimit: 100, usageCount: 45 },
      { code: "AI50", type: "PERCENTAGE", value: 50, minPurchase: 80, active: true, usageLimit: 50, usageCount: 12 },
      { code: "SAVE10", type: "FIXED", value: 10, minPurchase: 30, active: true, usageLimit: 200, usageCount: 88 },
      { code: "FLASH30", type: "PERCENTAGE", value: 30, minPurchase: 0, active: false, usageLimit: 30, usageCount: 30 },
    ];
    for (const c of couponData) {
      await ctx.db.insert("coupons", { ...c, expiresAt: undefined, vendorId: undefined });
    }

    return { seeded: true, message: "Demo data seeded successfully" };
  },
});import { query } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";

export const dashboard = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const [products, orders, vendors, reviews, notifications] = await Promise.all([
      ctx.db.query("products").collect(),
      ctx.db.query("orders").collect(),
      ctx.db.query("vendors").collect(),
      ctx.db.query("reviews").collect(),
      ctx.db.query("notifications").collect(),
    ]);

    const customers = new Set(orders.map((o) => o.customerEmail)).size;
    const revenue = orders
      .filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID")
      .reduce((s, o) => s + o.total, 0);
    const aov = orders.length > 0 ? revenue / orders.length : 0;
    const completedOrders = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID").length;
    const conversionRate = orders.length > 0 ? Math.round((completedOrders / orders.length) * 100 * 10) / 10 : 0;
    const avgRating =
      reviews.length > 0
        ? Math.round((reviews.reduce((s, r) => s + r.rating, 0) / reviews.length) * 10) / 10
        : 0;

    // Revenue timeseries (last 30 days using creation times)
    const now = Date.now();
    const revenueTimeseries = [];
    for (let i = 29; i >= 0; i--) {
      const dayMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
      const dayStart = now - i * dayMs;
      const dayEnd = dayStart + dayMs;
      const dayOrders = orders.filter(
        (o) => o._creationTime >= dayStart && o._creationTime < dayEnd &&
          (o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID")
      );
      const date = new Date(dayStart).toISOString().split("T")[0];
      revenueTimeseries.push({
        date,
        revenue: dayOrders.reduce((s, o) => s + o.total, 0),
        orders: dayOrders.length,
      });
    }

    // Revenue by category
    const catRevMap: Record<string, { name: string; revenue: number; orders: number }> = {};
    for (const order of orders) {
      if (order.status !== "COMPLETED" && order.status !== "PAID") continue;
      for (const item of order.items) {
        const product = products.find((p) => p._id === item.productId);
        const catId = product?.categoryId;
        if (!catId) continue;
        const cat = await ctx.db.get(catId);
        if (!cat) continue;
        if (!catRevMap[catId]) {
          catRevMap[catId] = { name: cat.name, revenue: 0, orders: 0 };
        }
        catRevMap[catId].revenue += item.price;
        catRevMap[catId].orders += 1;
      }
    }

    // Top products
    const topProducts = products
      .sort((a, b) => b.salesCount - a.salesCount)
      .slice(0, 5)
      .map((p) => ({
        title: p.title,
        sales: p.salesCount,
        revenue: p.price * p.salesCount,
        vendor: "—",
      }));

    // Top vendors
    const topVendors = vendors
      .sort((a, b) => b.totalRevenue - a.totalRevenue)
      .slice(0, 5)
      .map((v) => ({
        id: v._id,
        storeName: v.storeName,
        slug: v.slug,
        verified: v.verified,
        totalSales: v.totalSales,
        totalRevenue: v.totalRevenue,
        rating: v.rating,
      }));

    // Traffic sources (static for now)
    const trafficSources = [
      { source: "Organic Search", value: 38 },
      { source: "Direct", value: 25 },
      { source: "Social Media", value: 18 },
      { source: "Referral", value: 12 },
      { source: "Email", value: 7 },
    ];

    // Payment providers
    const providerCounts: Record<string, number> = {};
    for (const o of orders) {
      if (o.provider) {
        providerCounts[o.provider] = (providerCounts[o.provider] ?? 0) + 1;
      }
    }
    const paymentProviders = Object.entries(providerCounts).map(([name, value]) => ({ name, value }));

    return {
      summary: {
        revenue,
        liveRevenue: revenue,
        orders: orders.length,
        customers,
        products: products.length,
        vendors: vendors.length,
        reviews: reviews.length,
        aov,
        conversionRate,
        avgRating,
        paymentSuccessRate: Math.round((completedOrders / Math.max(1, orders.length)) * 100),
      },
      revenueTimeseries,
      revenueByCategory: Object.values(catRevMap),
      paymentProviders,
      topProducts,
      topVendors,
      trafficSources,
    };
  },
});
import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let products = await ctx.db.query("products").collect();

    if (args.status) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.type) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.type === args.type);
    }
    if (args.featured !== undefined) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.featured === args.featured);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      products = products.filter(
        (p) => p.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) || p.sku.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    // Attach vendor + category names
    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      products.map(async (p) => {
        const vendor = p.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(p.vendorId) : null;
        const category = p.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(p.categoryId) : null;
        return {
          ...p,
          vendorName: vendor?.storeName ?? null,
          categoryName: category?.name ?? null,
          effectivePrice: p.discountPrice ?? p.price,
          discountPercent: p.discountPrice ? Math.round(((p.price - p.discountPrice) / p.price) * 100) : 0,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const product = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!product) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Product not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    const vendor = product.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(product.vendorId) : null;
    const category = product.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(product.categoryId) : null;
    const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").withIndex("by_product", (q) => q.eq("productId", args.id)).collect();
    return { product: { ...product, vendorName: vendor?.storeName, categoryName: category?.name }, reviews };
  },
});

export const create = mutation({
  args: {
    title: v.string(),
    type: v.string(),
    price: v.number(),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    status: v.string(),
    featured: v.boolean(),
    shortDescription: v.optional(v.string()),
    vendorId: v.optional(v.id("vendors")),
    categoryId: v.optional(v.id("categories")),
    tags: v.array(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const slug = args.title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-") + "-" + Date.now();
    return await ctx.db.insert("products", {
      ...args,
      slug,
      description: args.shortDescription ?? "",
      currency: "USD",
      sku: `PB-${Date.now()}`,
      coverType: "gradient",
      coverColors: ["#3b82f6", "#8b5cf6"],
      tags: args.tags,
      rating: 0,
      reviewCount: 0,
      salesCount: 0,
      featured: args.featured,
    });
  },
});

export const update = mutation({
  args: {
    id: v.id("products"),
    title: v.optional(v.string()),
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    price: v.optional(v.number()),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const { id, ...updates } = args;
    const filtered = Object.fromEntries(
      Object.entries(updates).filter(([, v]) => v !== undefined)
    );
    await ctx.db.patch(id, filtered);
  },
});

export const remove = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.delete(args.id);
  },
});

export const pending = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const products = await ctx.db.query("products").withIndex("by_status", (q) => q.eq("status", "PENDING")).collect();
    return { items: products };
  },
});

export const approve = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "ACTIVE" });
  },
});

export const reject = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "REJECTED" });
  },
});

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let products = await ctx.db.query("products").collect();

    if (args.status) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.type) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.type === args.type);
    }
    if (args.featured !== undefined) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.featured === args.featured);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      products = products.filter(
        (p) => p.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) || p.sku.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    // Attach vendor + category names
    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      products.map(async (p) => {
        const vendor = p.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(p.vendorId) : null;

          ...p,

        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const product = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!product) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Product not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    const vendor = product.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(product.vendorId) : null;
    const category = product.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(product.categoryId) : null;
    const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").withIndex("by_product", (q) => q.eq("productId", args.id)).collect();
    return { product: { ...product, vendorName: vendor?.storeName, categoryName: category?.name }, reviews };
  },
});

import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    if (args.status) {
      orders = orders.filter((o) => o.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      orders = orders.filter(
        (o) =>
          o.orderNumber.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerName.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerEmail.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }
    return {
      items: orders.sort((a, b) => b._creationTime - a._creationTime),
    };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const order = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!order) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Order not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    return order;
  },
});

export const updateStatus = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders"), status: v.string() },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: args.status });
  },
});

export const refund = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "REFUNDED", paymentStatus: "REFUNDED" });
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    const total = orders.length;
    const completed = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID").length;
    const pending = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "PENDING").length;
    const refunded = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "REFUNDED").length;
    const revenue = orders
      .filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID")
      .reduce((s, o) => s + o.total, 0);
    return { total, completed, pending, refunded, revenue };
  },
});import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let products = await ctx.db.query("products").collect();

    if (args.status) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.type) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.type === args.type);
    }
    if (args.featured !== undefined) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.featured === args.featured);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      products = products.filter(
        (p) => p.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) || p.sku.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    // Attach vendor + category names
    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      products.map(async (p) => {
        const vendor = p.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(p.vendorId) : null;
        const category = p.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(p.categoryId) : null;
        return {
          ...p,
          vendorName: vendor?.storeName ?? null,
          categoryName: category?.name ?? null,
          effectivePrice: p.discountPrice ?? p.price,
          discountPercent: p.discountPrice ? Math.round(((p.price - p.discountPrice) / p.price) * 100) : 0,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const product = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!product) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Product not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    const vendor = product.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(product.vendorId) : null;
    const category = product.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(product.categoryId) : null;
    const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").withIndex("by_product", (q) => q.eq("productId", args.id)).collect();
    return { product: { ...product, vendorName: vendor?.storeName, categoryName: category?.name }, reviews };
  },
});

export const create = mutation({
  args: {
    title: v.string(),
    type: v.string(),
    price: v.number(),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    status: v.string(),
    featured: v.boolean(),
    shortDescription: v.optional(v.string()),
    vendorId: v.optional(v.id("vendors")),
    categoryId: v.optional(v.id("categories")),
    tags: v.array(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const slug = args.title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-") + "-" + Date.now();
    return await ctx.db.insert("products", {
      ...args,
      slug,
      description: args.shortDescription ?? "",
      currency: "USD",
      sku: `PB-${Date.now()}`,
      coverType: "gradient",
      coverColors: ["#3b82f6", "#8b5cf6"],
      tags: args.tags,
      rating: 0,
      reviewCount: 0,
      salesCount: 0,
      featured: args.featured,
    });
  },
});

export const update = mutation({
  args: {
    id: v.id("products"),
    title: v.optional(v.string()),
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    price: v.optional(v.number()),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const { id, ...updates } = args;
    const filtered = Object.fromEntries(
      Object.entries(updates).filter(([, v]) => v !== undefined)
    );
    await ctx.db.patch(id, filtered);
  },
});

export const remove = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.delete(args.id);
  },
});

export const pending = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const products = await ctx.db.query("products").withIndex("by_status", (q) => q.eq("status", "PENDING")).collect();
    return { items: products };
  },
});

export const approve = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "ACTIVE" });
  },
});

export const reject = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "REJECTED" });
  },
});
import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    if (args.status) {
      orders = orders.filter((o) => o.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      orders = orders.filter(
        (o) =>
          o.orderNumber.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerName.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerEmail.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }
    return {
      items: orders.sort((a, b) => b._creationTime - a._creationTime),
    };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const order = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!order) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Order not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    return order;
  },
});

export const updateStatus = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders"), status: v.string() },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: args.status });
  },
});

export const refund = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "REFUNDED", paymentStatus: "REFUNDED" });
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    const total = orders.length;
    const completed = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID").length;
    const pending = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "PENDING").length;
    const refunded = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "REFUNDED").length;
    const revenue = orders
      .filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID")
      .reduce((s, o) => s + o.total, 0);
    return { total, completed, pending, refunded, revenue };
  },
});
import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

// List all users with enriched vendor/affiliate info
export const listAdmin = query({
  args: {
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    role: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let users = await ctx.db.query("users").collect();

    if (args.role && args.role !== "ALL") {
      users = users.filter((u) => (u.role ?? "CUSTOMER") === args.role);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      users = users.filter(
        (u) =>
          (u.name ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          (u.email ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      users.map(async (u) => {
        const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").withIndex("by_customer", (q) => q.eq("customerId", u._id)).collect();
        const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").collect();
        const userReviews = reviews.filter((r) => r.authorId === u._id);
        const vendor = await ctx.db.query("vendors").filter((q) => q.eq(q.field("userId"), u._id)).first();
        const affiliate = await ctx.db.query("affiliates").withIndex("by_user", (q) => q.eq("userId", u._id)).first();

        return {
          id: u._id,
          name: u.name ?? "Unknown",
          email: u.email ?? "",
          role: u.role ?? "CUSTOMER",
          verified: u.verified ?? false,
          banned: u.banned ?? false,
          createdAt: new Date(u._creationTime).toISOString(),
          orderCount: orders.length,
          reviewCount: userReviews.length,
          vendor: vendor ? { storeName: vendor.storeName, totalRevenue: vendor.totalRevenue } : null,
          affiliate: affiliate ? { code: affiliate.code, earnings: affiliate.totalEarnings } : null,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

export const updateRole = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("users"), role: v.string() },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { role: args.role });
  },
});

export const verify = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("users") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { verified: true });
  },
});

export const ban = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("users") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { banned: true });
  },
});

  args: { id: v.id("users") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { banned: false });
  },
});

// Existing user sync from auth
export const updateCurrentUser = mutation({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const identity = await ctx.auth.getUserIdentity();
    if (!identity) return;
    const existing = await ctx.db
      .query("users")
      .withIndex("by_token", (q) => q.eq("tokenIdentifier", identity.tokenIdentifier))
      .unique();
    if (existing) {
      await ctx.db.patch(existing._id, {
        name: identity.name,
        email: identity.email,
      });
    } else {
      await ctx.db.insert("users", {
        tokenIdentifier: identity.tokenIdentifier,
        name: identity.name,
        email: identity.email,
        role: "CUSTOMER",
        verified: false,
      });
    }
  },
});

export const getCurrentUser = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const identity = await ctx.auth.getUserIdentity();
    if (!identity) return null;
    return await ctx.db
      .query("users")
      .withIndex("by_token", (q) => q.eq("tokenIdentifier", identity.tokenIdentifier))
      .unique();
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const users = await ctx.db.query("users").collect();
    const total = users.length;
    const admins = users.filter((u) => u.role === "ADMIN").length;
    const vendors = users.filter((u) => u.role === "VENDOR").length;
    const customers = users.filter((u) => !u.role || u.role === "CUSTOMER").length;
    const verified = users.filter((u) => u.verified).length;
    return { total, admins, vendors, customers, verified };
  },
});import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";

  args: {},

    const coupons = await ctx.db.query("coupons").collect();

export const create = mutation({
  args: {
    code: v.string(),
    type: v.string(),
    value: v.number(),
    minPurchase: v.number(),
    active: v.boolean(),
    usageLimit: v.optional(v.number()),
    expiresAt: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    // Check if code already exists
    const existing = await ctx.db.query("coupons").withIndex("by_code", (q) => q.eq("code", args.code)).first();
    if (existing) throw new Error("Coupon code already exists");
    return await ctx.db.insert("coupons", { ...args, usageCount: 0 });
  },
});

export const toggle = mutation({

  },

  args: {

  },

      products = products.filter((p) => p.featured === args.featured);
    }

      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      products = products.filter(
        (p) => p.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) || p.sku.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    // Attach vendor + category names
    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      products.map(async (p) => {
        const vendor = p.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(p.vendorId) : null;
        const category = p.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(p.categoryId) : null;
        return {
          ...p,
          vendorName: vendor?.storeName ?? null,
          categoryName: category?.name ?? null,
          effectivePrice: p.discountPrice ?? p.price,
          discountPercent: p.discountPrice ? Math.round(((p.price - p.discountPrice) / p.price) * 100) : 0,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const product = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!product) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Product not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    const vendor = product.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(product.vendorId) : null;
    const category = product.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(product.categoryId) : null;
    const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").withIndex("by_product", (q) => q.eq("productId", args.id)).collect();
    return { product: { ...product, vendorName: vendor?.storeName, categoryName: category?.name }, reviews };
  },
});

export const create = mutation({
  args: {
    title: v.string(),
    type: v.string(),
    price: v.number(),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    status: v.string(),
    featured: v.boolean(),
    shortDescription: v.optional(v.string()),
    vendorId: v.optional(v.id("vendors")),
    categoryId: v.optional(v.id("categories")),
    tags: v.array(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const slug = args.title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-") + "-" + Date.now();
    return await ctx.db.insert("products", {
      ...args,
      slug,
      description: args.shortDescription ?? "",
      currency: "USD",
      sku: `PB-${Date.now()}`,
      coverType: "gradient",
      coverColors: ["#3b82f6", "#8b5cf6"],
      tags: args.tags,
      rating: 0,
      reviewCount: 0,
      salesCount: 0,
      featured: args.featured,
    });
  },
});

export const update = mutation({
  args: {
    id: v.id("products"),
    title: v.optional(v.string()),
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    price: v.optional(v.number()),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const { id, ...updates } = args;
    const filtered = Object.fromEntries(
      Object.entries(updates).filter(([, v]) => v !== undefined)
    );
    await ctx.db.patch(id, filtered);
  },
});

export const remove = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },

  },
});

import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    if (args.status) {
      orders = orders.filter((o) => o.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      orders = orders.filter(
        (o) =>
          o.orderNumber.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerName.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerEmail.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }
    return {
      items: orders.sort((a, b) => b._creationTime - a._creationTime),
    };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const order = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!order) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Order not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    return order;
  },
});

export const updateStatus = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders"), status: v.string() },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: args.status });
  },
});

export const refund = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "REFUNDED", paymentStatus: "REFUNDED" });
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    const total = orders.length;
    const completed = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID").length;
    const pending = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "PENDING").length;
    const refunded = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "REFUNDED").length;
    const revenue = orders
      .filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID")
      .reduce((s, o) => s + o.total, 0);
    return { total, completed, pending, refunded, revenue };
  },
});
import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

// List all users with enriched vendor/affiliate info
export const listAdmin = query({
  args: {
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    role: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let users = await ctx.db.query("users").collect();

    if (args.role && args.role !== "ALL") {
      users = users.filter((u) => (u.role ?? "CUSTOMER") === args.role);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      users = users.filter(
        (u) =>
          (u.name ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          (u.email ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      users.map(async (u) => {
        const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").withIndex("by_customer", (q) => q.eq("customerId", u._id)).collect();
        const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").collect();
        const userReviews = reviews.filter((r) => r.authorId === u._id);
        const vendor = await ctx.db.query("vendors").filter((q) => q.eq(q.field("userId"), u._id)).first();
        const affiliate = await ctx.db.query("affiliates").withIndex("by_user", (q) => q.eq("userId", u._id)).first();

        return {
          id: u._id,
          name: u.name ?? "Unknown",
          email: u.email ?? "",
          role: u.role ?? "CUSTOMER",
          verified: u.verified ?? false,
          banned: u.banned ?? false,
          createdAt: new Date(u._creationTime).toISOString(),
          orderCount: orders.length,
          reviewCount: userReviews.length,
          vendor: vendor ? { storeName: vendor.storeName, totalRevenue: vendor.totalRevenue } : null,
          affiliate: affiliate ? { code: affiliate.code, earnings: affiliate.totalEarnings } : null,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

export const updateRole = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("users"), role: v.string() },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { role: args.role });
  },
});

export const verify = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("users") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { verified: true });
  },
});

export const ban = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("users") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { banned: true });
  },
});

export const unban = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("users") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { banned: false });
  },
});

// Existing user sync from auth
export const updateCurrentUser = mutation({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const identity = await ctx.auth.getUserIdentity();
    if (!identity) return;
    const existing = await ctx.db
      .query("users")
      .withIndex("by_token", (q) => q.eq("tokenIdentifier", identity.tokenIdentifier))
      .unique();
    if (existing) {
      await ctx.db.patch(existing._id, {
        name: identity.name,
        email: identity.email,
      });
    } else {
      await ctx.db.insert("users", {
        tokenIdentifier: identity.tokenIdentifier,
        name: identity.name,
        email: identity.email,
        role: "CUSTOMER",
        verified: false,
      });
    }
  },
});

export const getCurrentUser = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const identity = await ctx.auth.getUserIdentity();
    if (!identity) return null;
    return await ctx.db
      .query("users")
      .withIndex("by_token", (q) => q.eq("tokenIdentifier", identity.tokenIdentifier))
      .unique();
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const users = await ctx.db.query("users").collect();
    const total = users.length;
    const admins = users.filter((u) => u.role === "ADMIN").length;
    const vendors = users.filter((u) => u.role === "VENDOR").length;
    const customers = users.filter((u) => !u.role || u.role === "CUSTOMER").length;
    const verified = users.filter((u) => u.verified).length;
    return { total, admins, vendors, customers, verified };
  },
});
import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";

  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const coupons = await ctx.db.query("coupons").collect();

  },
});

export const create = mutation({
  args: {
    code: v.string(),
    type: v.string(),
    value: v.number(),
    minPurchase: v.number(),
    active: v.boolean(),
    usageLimit: v.optional(v.number()),
    expiresAt: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    // Check if code already exists
    const existing = await ctx.db.query("coupons").withIndex("by_code", (q) => q.eq("code", args.code)).first();
    if (existing) throw new Error("Coupon code already exists");
    return await ctx.db.insert("coupons", { ...args, usageCount: 0 });
  },
});

  },
});

    minPurchase: v.optional(v.number()),
    active: v.optional(v.boolean()),
    usageLimit: v.optional(v.number()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const { id, ...updates } = args;
    const filtered = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(updates).filter(([, v]) => v !== undefined));
    await ctx.db.patch(id, filtered);
  },
});

export const markAllRead = mutation({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const unread = await ctx.db.query("notifications").withIndex("by_read", (q) => q.eq("read", false)).collect();
    for (const n of unread) {
      await ctx.db.patch(n._id, { read: true });
    }
  },
});

import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let products = await ctx.db.query("products").collect();

    if (args.status) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.type) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.type === args.type);
    }
    if (args.featured !== undefined) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.featured === args.featured);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      products = products.filter(
        (p) => p.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) || p.sku.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    // Attach vendor + category names
    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      products.map(async (p) => {
        const vendor = p.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(p.vendorId) : null;
        const category = p.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(p.categoryId) : null;
        return {
          ...p,
          vendorName: vendor?.storeName ?? null,
          categoryName: category?.name ?? null,
          effectivePrice: p.discountPrice ?? p.price,
          discountPercent: p.discountPrice ? Math.round(((p.price - p.discountPrice) / p.price) * 100) : 0,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const product = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!product) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Product not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    const vendor = product.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(product.vendorId) : null;
    const category = product.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(product.categoryId) : null;
    const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").withIndex("by_product", (q) => q.eq("productId", args.id)).collect();
    return { product: { ...product, vendorName: vendor?.storeName, categoryName: category?.name }, reviews };
  },
});

    const admins = users.filter((u) => u.role === "ADMIN").length;
    const vendors = users.filter((u) => u.role === "VENDOR").length;
    const customers = users.filter((u) => !u.role || u.role === "CUSTOMER").length;
    const verified = users.filter((u) => u.verified).length;
    return { total, admins, vendors, customers, verified };
  },
});

  args: {
    code: v.string(),
    type: v.string(),
    value: v.number(),
    minPurchase: v.number(),
    active: v.boolean(),
    usageLimit: v.optional(v.number()),
    expiresAt: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    // Check if code already exists
    const existing = await ctx.db.query("coupons").withIndex("by_code", (q) => q.eq("code", args.code)).first();
    if (existing) throw new Error("Coupon code already exists");
    return await ctx.db.insert("coupons", { ...args, usageCount: 0 });
  },
});

export const list = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const settings = await ctx.db.query("settings").collect();

    for (const s of settings) {
      map[s.key] = s.value;
    }
    return { settings: map, items: settings };
  },
});

export const set = mutation({
  args: { key: v.string(), value: v.string(), category: v.optional(v.string()) },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const existing = await ctx.db.query("settings").withIndex("by_key", (q) => q.eq("key", args.key)).first();
    if (existing) {
      await ctx.db.patch(existing._id, { value: args.value });
    } else {
      await ctx.db.insert("settings", {
        key: args.key,
        value: args.value,
        category: args.category ?? "general",
      });
    }
  },
});

export const setBatch = mutation({
  args: { settings: v.array(v.object({ key: v.string(), value: v.string(), category: v.optional(v.string()) })) },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    for (const s of args.settings) {
      const existing = await ctx.db.query("settings").withIndex("by_key", (q) => q.eq("key", s.key)).first();
      if (existing) {
        await ctx.db.patch(existing._id, { value: s.value });
      } else {
        await ctx.db.insert("settings", { key: s.key, value: s.value, category: s.category ?? "general" });
      }
    }
  },
});
import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let products = await ctx.db.query("products").collect();

    if (args.status) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.type) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.type === args.type);
    }
    if (args.featured !== undefined) {
      products = products.filter((p) => p.featured === args.featured);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      products = products.filter(
        (p) => p.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) || p.sku.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    // Attach vendor + category names
    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      products.map(async (p) => {
        const vendor = p.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(p.vendorId) : null;
        const category = p.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(p.categoryId) : null;
        return {
          ...p,
          vendorName: vendor?.storeName ?? null,
          categoryName: category?.name ?? null,
          effectivePrice: p.discountPrice ?? p.price,
          discountPercent: p.discountPrice ? Math.round(((p.price - p.discountPrice) / p.price) * 100) : 0,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const product = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!product) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Product not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    const vendor = product.vendorId ? await ctx.db.get(product.vendorId) : null;
    const category = product.categoryId ? await ctx.db.get(product.categoryId) : null;
    const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").withIndex("by_product", (q) => q.eq("productId", args.id)).collect();
    return { product: { ...product, vendorName: vendor?.storeName, categoryName: category?.name }, reviews };
  },
});

export const create = mutation({
  args: {
    title: v.string(),
    type: v.string(),
    price: v.number(),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    status: v.string(),
    featured: v.boolean(),
    shortDescription: v.optional(v.string()),
    vendorId: v.optional(v.id("vendors")),
    categoryId: v.optional(v.id("categories")),
    tags: v.array(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const slug = args.title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-") + "-" + Date.now();
    return await ctx.db.insert("products", {
      ...args,
      slug,
      description: args.shortDescription ?? "",
      currency: "USD",
      sku: `PB-${Date.now()}`,
      coverType: "gradient",
      coverColors: ["#3b82f6", "#8b5cf6"],
      tags: args.tags,
      rating: 0,
      reviewCount: 0,
      salesCount: 0,
      featured: args.featured,
    });
  },
});

export const update = mutation({
  args: {
    id: v.id("products"),
    title: v.optional(v.string()),
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    price: v.optional(v.number()),

  },

    const { id, ...updates } = args;
    const filtered = Object.fromEntries(
      Object.entries(updates).filter(([, v]) => v !== undefined)
    );

  },
});

import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    if (args.status) {
      orders = orders.filter((o) => o.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      orders = orders.filter(
        (o) =>
          o.orderNumber.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerName.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerEmail.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }
    return {
      items: orders.sort((a, b) => b._creationTime - a._creationTime),
    };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const order = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!order) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Order not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    return order;
  },
});

export const updateStatus = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders"), status: v.string() },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: args.status });
  },
});

export const refund = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "REFUNDED", paymentStatus: "REFUNDED" });
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    const total = orders.length;
    const completed = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID").length;
    const pending = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "PENDING").length;
    const refunded = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "REFUNDED").length;
    const revenue = orders
      .filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID")
      .reduce((s, o) => s + o.total, 0);
    return { total, completed, pending, refunded, revenue };
  },
});
import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

// List all users with enriched vendor/affiliate info
export const listAdmin = query({
  args: {
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    role: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let users = await ctx.db.query("users").collect();

    if (args.role && args.role !== "ALL") {
      users = users.filter((u) => (u.role ?? "CUSTOMER") === args.role);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      users = users.filter(
        (u) =>
          (u.name ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          (u.email ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      users.map(async (u) => {
        const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").withIndex("by_customer", (q) => q.eq("customerId", u._id)).collect();
        const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").collect();
        const userReviews = reviews.filter((r) => r.authorId === u._id);
        const vendor = await ctx.db.query("vendors").filter((q) => q.eq(q.field("userId"), u._id)).first();
        const affiliate = await ctx.db.query("affiliates").withIndex("by_user", (q) => q.eq("userId", u._id)).first();

        return {
          id: u._id,
          name: u.name ?? "Unknown",
          email: u.email ?? "",
          role: u.role ?? "CUSTOMER",
          verified: u.verified ?? false,
          banned: u.banned ?? false,
          createdAt: new Date(u._creationTime).toISOString(),
          orderCount: orders.length,
          reviewCount: userReviews.length,
          vendor: vendor ? { storeName: vendor.storeName, totalRevenue: vendor.totalRevenue } : null,
          affiliate: affiliate ? { code: affiliate.code, earnings: affiliate.totalEarnings } : null,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { role: args.role });

// Existing user sync from auth
export const updateCurrentUser = mutation({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const identity = await ctx.auth.getUserIdentity();
    if (!identity) return;
    const existing = await ctx.db
      .query("users")
      .withIndex("by_token", (q) => q.eq("tokenIdentifier", identity.tokenIdentifier))
      .unique();
    if (existing) {
      await ctx.db.patch(existing._id, {
        name: identity.name,
        email: identity.email,
      });
    } else {
      await ctx.db.insert("users", {
        tokenIdentifier: identity.tokenIdentifier,
        name: identity.name,
        email: identity.email,
        role: "CUSTOMER",
        verified: false,
      });
    }
  },
});

export const getCurrentUser = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const identity = await ctx.auth.getUserIdentity();
    if (!identity) return null;
    return await ctx.db
      .query("users")
      .withIndex("by_token", (q) => q.eq("tokenIdentifier", identity.tokenIdentifier))
      .unique();
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const users = await ctx.db.query("users").collect();
    const total = users.length;
    const admins = users.filter((u) => u.role === "ADMIN").length;
    const vendors = users.filter((u) => u.role === "VENDOR").length;
    const customers = users.filter((u) => !u.role || u.role === "CUSTOMER").length;
    const verified = users.filter((u) => u.verified).length;
    return { total, admins, vendors, customers, verified };
  },
});

    type: v.string(),
    price: v.number(),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    status: v.string(),
    featured: v.boolean(),
    shortDescription: v.optional(v.string()),
    vendorId: v.optional(v.id("vendors")),
    categoryId: v.optional(v.id("categories")),
    tags: v.array(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const slug = args.title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "-") + "-" + Date.now();
    return await ctx.db.insert("products", {
      ...args,
      slug,
      description: args.shortDescription ?? "",
      currency: "USD",
      sku: `PB-${Date.now()}`,
      coverType: "gradient",
      coverColors: ["#3b82f6", "#8b5cf6"],
      tags: args.tags,
      rating: 0,
      reviewCount: 0,
      salesCount: 0,
      featured: args.featured,
    });
  },
});

export const update = mutation({
  args: {
    id: v.id("products"),
    title: v.optional(v.string()),
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    price: v.optional(v.number()),
    discountPrice: v.optional(v.number()),
    featured: v.optional(v.boolean()),
    type: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const { id, ...updates } = args;
    const filtered = Object.fromEntries(
      Object.entries(updates).filter(([, v]) => v !== undefined)
    );
    await ctx.db.patch(id, filtered);
  },
});

export const remove = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("products") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.delete(args.id);
  },
});

import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {
    status: v.optional(v.string()),
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    if (args.status) {
      orders = orders.filter((o) => o.status === args.status);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      orders = orders.filter(
        (o) =>
          o.orderNumber.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerName.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          o.customerEmail.toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }
    return {
      items: orders.sort((a, b) => b._creationTime - a._creationTime),
    };
  },
});

export const get = query({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const order = await ctx.db.get(args.id);
    if (!order) throw new ConvexError({ message: "Order not found", code: "NOT_FOUND" });
    return order;
  },
});

export const updateStatus = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders"), status: v.string() },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: args.status });
  },
});

export const refund = mutation({
  args: { id: v.id("orders") },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    await ctx.db.patch(args.id, { status: "REFUNDED", paymentStatus: "REFUNDED" });
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").collect();
    const total = orders.length;
    const completed = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID").length;
    const pending = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "PENDING").length;
    const refunded = orders.filter((o) => o.status === "REFUNDED").length;
    const revenue = orders
      .filter((o) => o.status === "COMPLETED" || o.status === "PAID")
      .reduce((s, o) => s + o.total, 0);
    return { total, completed, pending, refunded, revenue };
  },
});
import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";
import { ConvexError } from "convex/values";

// List all users with enriched vendor/affiliate info
export const listAdmin = query({
  args: {
    search: v.optional(v.string()),
    role: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    let users = await ctx.db.query("users").collect();

    if (args.role && args.role !== "ALL") {
      users = users.filter((u) => (u.role ?? "CUSTOMER") === args.role);
    }
    if (args.search) {
      const q = args.search.toLowerCase();
      users = users.filter(
        (u) =>
          (u.name ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          (u.email ?? "").toLowerCase().includes(q)
      );
    }

    const enriched = await Promise.all(
      users.map(async (u) => {
        const orders = await ctx.db.query("orders").withIndex("by_customer", (q) => q.eq("customerId", u._id)).collect();
        const reviews = await ctx.db.query("reviews").collect();
        const userReviews = reviews.filter((r) => r.authorId === u._id);
        const vendor = await ctx.db.query("vendors").filter((q) => q.eq(q.field("userId"), u._id)).first();
        const affiliate = await ctx.db.query("affiliates").withIndex("by_user", (q) => q.eq("userId", u._id)).first();

        return {
          id: u._id,
          name: u.name ?? "Unknown",
          email: u.email ?? "",
          role: u.role ?? "CUSTOMER",
          verified: u.verified ?? false,
          banned: u.banned ?? false,
          createdAt: new Date(u._creationTime).toISOString(),
          orderCount: orders.length,
          reviewCount: userReviews.length,
          vendor: vendor ? { storeName: vendor.storeName, totalRevenue: vendor.totalRevenue } : null,
          affiliate: affiliate ? { code: affiliate.code, earnings: affiliate.totalEarnings } : null,
        };
      })
    );

    return { items: enriched };
  },
});

// Existing user sync from auth
export const updateCurrentUser = mutation({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const identity = await ctx.auth.getUserIdentity();
    if (!identity) return;
    const existing = await ctx.db
      .query("users")
      .withIndex("by_token", (q) => q.eq("tokenIdentifier", identity.tokenIdentifier))
      .unique();
    if (existing) {
      await ctx.db.patch(existing._id, {
        name: identity.name,
        email: identity.email,
      });
    } else {
      await ctx.db.insert("users", {
        tokenIdentifier: identity.tokenIdentifier,
        name: identity.name,
        email: identity.email,
        role: "CUSTOMER",
        verified: false,
      });
    }
  },
});

export const getCurrentUser = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const identity = await ctx.auth.getUserIdentity();
    if (!identity) return null;
    return await ctx.db
      .query("users")
      .withIndex("by_token", (q) => q.eq("tokenIdentifier", identity.tokenIdentifier))
      .unique();
  },
});

export const stats = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const users = await ctx.db.query("users").collect();
    const total = users.length;
    const admins = users.filter((u) => u.role === "ADMIN").length;
    const vendors = users.filter((u) => u.role === "VENDOR").length;
    const customers = users.filter((u) => !u.role || u.role === "CUSTOMER").length;
    const verified = users.filter((u) => u.verified).length;
    return { total, admins, vendors, customers, verified };
  },
});

export const create = mutation({
  args: {
    code: v.string(),
    type: v.string(),
    value: v.number(),
    minPurchase: v.number(),
    active: v.boolean(),
    usageLimit: v.optional(v.number()),
    expiresAt: v.optional(v.string()),
  },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    // Check if code already exists
    const existing = await ctx.db.query("coupons").withIndex("by_code", (q) => q.eq("code", args.code)).first();
    if (existing) throw new Error("Coupon code already exists");
    return await ctx.db.insert("coupons", { ...args, usageCount: 0 });
  },
});

import { query, mutation } from "./_generated/server";
import { v } from "convex/values";

export const list = query({
  args: {},
  handler: async (ctx) => {
    const settings = await ctx.db.query("settings").collect();
    const map: Record<string, string> = {};
    for (const s of settings) {
      map[s.key] = s.value;
    }
    return { settings: map, items: settings };
  },
});

export const set = mutation({
  args: { key: v.string(), value: v.string(), category: v.optional(v.string()) },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    const existing = await ctx.db.query("settings").withIndex("by_key", (q) => q.eq("key", args.key)).first();
    if (existing) {
      await ctx.db.patch(existing._id, { value: args.value });
    } else {
      await ctx.db.insert("settings", {
        key: args.key,
        value: args.value,
        category: args.category ?? "general",
      });
    }
  },
});

export const setBatch = mutation({
  args: { settings: v.array(v.object({ key: v.string(), value: v.string(), category: v.optional(v.string()) })) },
  handler: async (ctx, args) => {
    for (const s of args.settings) {
      const existing = await ctx.db.query("settings").withIndex("by_key", (q) => q.eq("key", s.key)).first();
      if (existing) {
        await ctx.db.patch(existing._id, { value: s.value });
      } else {
        await ctx.db.insert("settings", { key: s.key, value: s.value, category: s.category ?? "general" });
      }
    }
  },
});

import { create } from "zustand";
import { persist } from "zustand/middleware";

type AdminUser = {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  role: string;
};

type ModuleKey =
  | "dashboard"
  | "analytics"
  | "products"
  | "orders"
  | "woocommerce"
  | "wordpress"
  | "jazzcash"
  | "subscriptions"
  | "coupons"
  | "users"
  | "support"
  | "iptv"
  | "finance"
  | "payments"
  | "reports"
  | "marketing"
  | "media"
  | "website"
  | "seo"
  | "ai"
  | "developer"
  | "integrations"
  | "security"
  | "settings"
  | "mobile";

interface AdminStore {
  user: AdminUser | null;
  setUser: (u: AdminUser | null) => void;
  activeModule: ModuleKey;
  setModule: (m: ModuleKey) => void;
}

export const useAdminStore = create<AdminStore>()(
  persist(
    (set) => ({
      user: null,
      setUser: (u) => set({ user: u }),
      activeModule: "dashboard",
      setModule: (m) => set({ activeModule: m }),
    }),
    {
      name: "playbeat-admin",
      partialize: (state) => ({ user: state.user, activeModule: state.activeModule }),
    }
  )
);

          {/* ADD ALL CUSTOM ROUTES ABOVE THE CATCH-ALL "*" ROUTE */}
          <Route path="*" element={<NotFound />} />

export default function AdminPage() {
  const { user, setUser } = useAdminStore();

  if (user?.role === "ADMIN") {
    return <AdminConsole />;

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen flex-col items-center justify-center bg-background px-4 py-10">
      <AdminLock
        onUnlock={(u) => {
          setUser(u);
          toast.success(`Welcome back, ${u.name}`);
        }}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

function AdminLock({ onUnlock }: { onUnlock: (u: { id: string; name: string; email: string; role: string }) => void }) {
  const [password, setPassword] = React.useState("");
  const [showPw, setShowPw] = React.useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = React.useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = React.useState("");

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError("");
    if (!password) { setError("Password is required."); return; }
    if (password !== ADMIN_PASSWORD) { setError("Incorrect password. Access denied."); return; }
    setLoading(true);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onUnlock({ id: "exec_admin", name: "Founder", email: "founder@playbeat.live", role: "ADMIN" });
      setLoading(false);
    }, 500);
  };

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.4 }}
      className="w-full max-w-sm"
    >
      {/* Ambient glow */}
      <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 overflow-hidden">
        <div className="absolute left-1/2 top-1/4 size-96 -translate-x-1/2 rounded-full bg-primary/10 blur-3xl" />
      </div>

      <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-card/80 backdrop-blur-xl">
        <div className="h-0.5 w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary via-accent to-primary" />

        <div className="p-8">
          {/* Logo */}
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 text-center">
            <div className="flex size-16 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/20 to-accent/20 border border-white/10">
              <Zap className="size-8 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <Lock className="size-3.5 text-accent" />
              <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.25em] text-accent">
                Restricted Access
              </span>
            </div>
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold tracking-tight">
              <span className="text-foreground">Play</span>
              <span className="bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent bg-clip-text text-transparent">Beat</span>
            </h1>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
              Admin Portal — enter your password to access the platform console.
            </p>
          </div>

          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="mt-7 space-y-4">
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label htmlFor="admin-pw" className="text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">
                Admin Password
              </Label>
              <div className="relative">
                <KeyRound className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 size-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground" />
                <Input
                  id="admin-pw"
                  type={showPw ? "text" : "password"}
                  value={password}
                  onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                  placeholder="••••••••••••"
                  className="h-11 border-white/10 bg-white/5 pl-9 pr-9"
                  autoComplete="current-password"
                  autoFocus
                />
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => setShowPw((s) => !s)}
                  className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
                  aria-label={showPw ? "Hide" : "Show"}
                >
                  {showPw ? <EyeOff className="size-4" /> : <Eye className="size-4" />}
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {error && (
              <div className="rounded-lg border border-destructive/30 bg-destructive/10 px-3 py-2 text-xs text-destructive">
                {error}
              </div>
            )}

            <Button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="h-11 w-full gap-2 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent hover:opacity-90 text-white font-semibold">
              {loading ? (
                <Loader2 className="size-4 animate-spin" />
              ) : (
                <>
                  <Shield className="size-4" />
                  Unlock Admin Access
                  <ArrowRight className="size-4" />
                </>
              )}
            </Button>
          </form>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="mt-5 flex items-center justify-center gap-5 text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">
        <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><ShieldCheck className="size-3 text-primary" /> Secure</span>
        <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><Lock className="size-3 text-accent" /> Encrypted</span>
        <Badge variant="outline" className="border-white/10 text-[9px] uppercase tracking-wider">Exec Only</Badge>
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
}

function SidebarContent({
  active, onSelect, onClose,
}: {
  active: ModuleKey;
  onSelect: (k: ModuleKey) => void;
  onClose?: () => void;
}) {
  const { user, setUser } = useAdminStore();

  return (
    <div className="flex h-full flex-col overflow-hidden">
      {/* Logo */}
      <div className="flex h-16 shrink-0 items-center gap-3 border-b border-white/8 px-5">
        <div className="flex size-8 items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/30 to-accent/30">
          <Zap className="size-4 text-primary" />
        </div>
        <span className="text-base font-bold tracking-tight">
          <span className="text-foreground">Play</span>
          <span className="bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent bg-clip-text text-transparent">Beat</span>
        </span>
        <Badge className="ml-auto bg-primary/15 text-primary text-[9px] uppercase tracking-wider">Admin</Badge>
      </div>

      {/* Nav */}
      <nav className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto scrollbar-thin px-3 py-3">
        {NAV_GROUPS.map((group) => (
          <div key={group.label} className="mb-3">
            <p className="px-3 pb-1 text-[9px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground/50">
              {group.label}
            </p>
            {group.items.map((item) => {
              const Icon = item.icon;
              const isActive = active === item.key;
              return (
                <button
                  key={item.key}
                  onClick={() => { onSelect(item.key); onClose?.(); }}
                  className={cn(
                    "flex w-full items-center gap-2.5 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition-all cursor-pointer",
                    isActive
                      ? "bg-gradient-to-r from-primary/15 to-accent/10 text-foreground"
                      : "text-muted-foreground hover:bg-white/5 hover:text-foreground"
                  )}
                >
                  <Icon className={cn("size-3.5 shrink-0", isActive ? "text-primary" : "")} />
                  <span className="truncate">{item.label}</span>
                  {isActive && <ChevronRight className="ml-auto size-3 text-primary" />}
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        ))}
      </nav>

      {/* User footer */}
      <div className="shrink-0 border-t border-white/8 p-3">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5 rounded-lg bg-white/5 p-2.5">
          <div className="grid size-7 place-items-center rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/30 to-accent/30 text-xs font-bold text-primary">
            {user?.name?.charAt(0) ?? "A"}
          </div>
          <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
            <p className="truncate text-xs font-semibold">{user?.name ?? "Admin"}</p>
            <p className="truncate text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{user?.email ?? ""}</p>
          </div>
          <Button
            size="icon"
            variant="ghost"
            className="size-7 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive"
            onClick={() => { setUser(null); toast.success("Signed out"); }}
          >
            <LogOut className="size-3.5" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function AdminConsole() {
  const { activeModule, setModule } = useAdminStore();
  const [mobileOpen, setMobileOpen] = React.useState(false);
  const notifCount = useQuery(api.notifications.unreadCount);

  const renderModule = () => {
    switch (activeModule) {
      case "dashboard": return <AdminDashboard />;
      case "users": return <AdminUsers />;
      case "products": return <AdminProducts />;
      case "orders": return <AdminOrders />;
      case "coupons": return <AdminCoupons />;
      case "settings": return <AdminSettings />;
      case "payments": return <AdminPayments />;
      case "reports": return <AdminReports />;
      case "marketing": return <AdminMarketing />;
      case "security": return <AdminSecurity />;
      default: {
        const mod = SIMPLE_MODULES[activeModule];
        if (mod) {
          return <SimpleModule title={mod.title} description={mod.description} icon={mod.icon} features={mod.features} />;
        }
        return <AdminDashboard />;
      }
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen bg-background">
      {/* Desktop sidebar */}
      <aside className="fixed inset-y-0 left-0 z-30 hidden w-56 border-r border-white/8 bg-sidebar lg:flex lg:flex-col">
        <SidebarContent active={activeModule} onSelect={setModule} />
      </aside>

      {/* Mobile sidebar */}
      <Sheet open={mobileOpen} onOpenChange={setMobileOpen}>
        <SheetContent side="left" className="w-56 border-r border-white/8 bg-sidebar p-0">
          <SidebarContent active={activeModule} onSelect={setModule} onClose={() => setMobileOpen(false)} />
        </SheetContent>
      </Sheet>

      {/* Main area */}
      <div className="flex flex-1 flex-col lg:pl-56">
        {/* Topbar */}
        <header className="sticky top-0 z-20 flex h-14 items-center gap-3 border-b border-white/8 bg-background/80 px-4 backdrop-blur-xl sm:px-6">
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="size-8 lg:hidden" onClick={() => setMobileOpen(true)}>
            <Menu className="size-4" />
          </Button>

          <div className="relative hidden max-w-xs flex-1 sm:flex">
            <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 size-3.5 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground" />
            <Input placeholder="Search admin..." className="h-8 border-white/10 bg-white/5 pl-8 text-sm" />
          </div>

          <div className="ml-auto flex items-center gap-2">
            <SeedButton />
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="relative size-8">
              <Bell className="size-4" />
              {(notifCount?.count ?? 0) > 0 && (
                <span className="absolute right-1 top-1 flex size-2 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-primary text-[8px] font-bold text-white" />
              )}
            </Button>
            <Badge className="hidden bg-gradient-to-r from-primary/20 to-accent/20 text-primary border-primary/20 sm:flex text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider">
              Admin
            </Badge>
          </div>
        </header>

        {/* Module content */}
        <main className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4 sm:p-6">
          <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
            <motion.div
              key={activeModule}
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
              transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
            >
              {renderModule()}
            </motion.div>
          </AnimatePresence>
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
Now let me build all the core modules:
