  const [mobileOpen, setMobileOpen] = React.useState(false);
  const notifCount = useQuery(api.notifications.unreadCount);

  const renderModule = () => {
    switch (activeModule) {
      case "dashboard": return <AdminDashboard />;
      case "users": return <AdminUsers />;
      case "products": return <AdminProducts />;
      case "orders": return <AdminOrders />;
      case "coupons": return <AdminCoupons />;
      case "settings": return <AdminSettings />;
      case "payments": return <AdminPayments />;
      case "reports": return <AdminReports />;
      case "marketing": return <AdminMarketing />;
      case "security": return <AdminSecurity />;
      default: {
        const mod = SIMPLE_MODULES[activeModule];
        if (mod) {
          return <SimpleModule title={mod.title} description={mod.description} icon={mod.icon} features={mod.features} />;
        }
        return <AdminDashboard />;
      }
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen bg-background">
      {/* Desktop sidebar */}
      <aside className="fixed inset-y-0 left-0 z-30 hidden w-56 border-r border-white/8 bg-sidebar lg:flex lg:flex-col">
        <SidebarContent active={activeModule} onSelect={setModule} />
      </aside>

      {/* Mobile sidebar */}
      <Sheet open={mobileOpen} onOpenChange={setMobileOpen}>
        <SheetContent side="left" className="w-56 border-r border-white/8 bg-sidebar p-0">
          <SidebarContent active={activeModule} onSelect={setModule} onClose={() => setMobileOpen(false)} />
        </SheetContent>
      </Sheet>

      {/* Main area */}
      <div className="flex flex-1 flex-col lg:pl-56">
        {/* Topbar */}
        <header className="sticky top-0 z-20 flex h-14 items-center gap-3 border-b border-white/8 bg-background/80 px-4 backdrop-blur-xl sm:px-6">
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="size-8 lg:hidden" onClick={() => setMobileOpen(true)}>
            <Menu className="size-4" />
          </Button>

          <div className="relative hidden max-w-xs flex-1 sm:flex">
            <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 size-3.5 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground" />
            <Input placeholder="Search admin..." className="h-8 border-white/10 bg-white/5 pl-8 text-sm" />
          </div>

          <div className="ml-auto flex items-center gap-2">
            <SeedButton />
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="relative size-8">
              <Bell className="size-4" />
              {(notifCount?.count ?? 0) > 0 && (
                <span className="absolute right-1 top-1 flex size-2 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-primary text-[8px] font-bold text-white" />
              )}
            </Button>
            <Badge className="hidden bg-gradient-to-r from-primary/20 to-accent/20 text-primary border-primary/20 sm:flex text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider">
              Admin
            </Badge>
          </div>
        </header>

        {/* Module content */}
        <main className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4 sm:p-6">
          <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
            <motion.div
              key={activeModule}
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
              transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
            >
              {renderModule()}
            </motion.div>
          </AnimatePresence>
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
Now let me build all the core modules:

import * as React from "react";
import { motion } from "motion/react";
import { useQuery, useQueryClient } from "convex/react";
import {
  DollarSign, Users, ShoppingCart, Package, CreditCard, TrendingUp,
  TrendingDown, Activity, Server, Globe, Zap, Bell, RefreshCw,
} from "lucide-react";
import {
  Area, AreaChart, Bar, BarChart, Cell, Pie, PieChart,
  ResponsiveContainer, Tooltip, XAxis, YAxis, CartesianGrid,
} from "recharts";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card.tsx";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge.tsx";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button.tsx";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton.tsx";
import { api } from "@/convex/_generated/api.js";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils.ts";

const CHART_COLORS = ["#3b82f6", "#8b5cf6", "#ec4899", "#06b6d4", "#10b981"];

function fmt(n: number) {
  return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US", { style: "currency", currency: "USD", maximumFractionDigits: 0 }).format(n);
}
function fmtDate(iso: string) {
  try { return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("en-US", { month: "short", day: "numeric" }).format(new Date(iso)); }
  catch { return iso; }
}

function KpiCard({ icon: Icon, label, value, trend, accent = false, delay = 0 }: {
  icon: React.ElementType; label: string; value: string;
  trend?: { value: string; up: boolean }; accent?: boolean; delay?: number;
}) {
  return (
    <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay }}>
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60 backdrop-blur">
        <CardContent className="p-4">
          <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
            <div className="min-w-0">
              <p className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">{label}</p>
              <p className="mt-1 text-xl font-bold leading-none">{value}</p>
              {trend && (
                <div className="mt-1.5 flex items-center gap-1 text-xs">
                  {trend.up ? <TrendingUp className="size-3 text-green-400" /> : <TrendingDown className="size-3 text-red-400" />}
                  <span className={trend.up ? "text-green-400" : "text-red-400"}>{trend.value}</span>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
            <div className={cn(
              "shrink-0 grid size-9 place-items-center rounded-xl",
              accent ? "bg-accent/15" : "bg-primary/15"
            )}>
              <Icon className={cn("size-4", accent ? "text-accent" : "text-primary")} />
            </div>
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </motion.div>
  );
}

function ChartTip({ active, payload, label }: { active?: boolean; payload?: Array<{ name: string; value: number; color: string }>; label?: string }) {
  if (!active || !payload?.length) return null;
  return (
    <div className="rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-black/80 px-3 py-2 text-xs backdrop-blur-xl">
      <p className="mb-1 font-medium">{label}</p>
      {payload.map((p, i) => (
        <p key={i} style={{ color: p.color }}>{p.name}: {p.value.toLocaleString()}</p>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

export function AdminDashboard() {
  const qc = useQueryClient();
  const dash = useQuery(api.analytics.dashboard);
  const orders = useQuery(api.orders.list, {});
  const notifs = useQuery(api.notifications.list);
  const isLoading = dash === undefined;

  const summary = dash?.summary;
  const recentOrders = (orders?.items ?? []).slice(0, 6);
  const notifications = (notifs?.items ?? []).slice(0, 5);
  const revenueData = (dash?.revenueTimeseries ?? []).slice(-14);
  const trafficData = dash?.trafficSources ?? [];
  const topProducts = dash?.topProducts ?? [];

  const statusColor: Record<string, string> = {
    COMPLETED: "bg-green-500/15 text-green-400",
    PAID: "bg-blue-500/15 text-blue-400",
    PENDING: "bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-400",
    REFUNDED: "bg-red-500/15 text-red-400",
    CANCELLED: "bg-gray-500/15 text-gray-400",
  };

  const refresh = () => {
    qc.invalidateQueries();
    toast.success("Dashboard refreshed");
  };

  return (
    <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="space-y-5">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Dashboard</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Real-time overview of your PlayBeat marketplace</p>
        </div>
        <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="gap-1.5 border-white/10 bg-white/5" onClick={refresh}>
          <RefreshCw className="size-3.5" /> Refresh
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* KPI cards */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-6">
        {isLoading ? Array.from({ length: 6 }).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-24 rounded-xl" />) : (
          <>
            <KpiCard icon={DollarSign} label="Revenue" value={summary ? fmt(summary.revenue) : "—"} trend={{ value: "+12.5%", up: true }} delay={0} />
            <KpiCard icon={Users} label="Customers" value={summary ? String(summary.customers) : "—"} trend={{ value: "+8.2%", up: true }} delay={0.05} />
            <KpiCard icon={ShoppingCart} label="Orders" value={summary ? String(summary.orders) : "—"} trend={{ value: "+15.3%", up: true }} delay={0.1} />
            <KpiCard icon={Package} label="Products" value={summary ? String(summary.products) : "—"} delay={0.15} />
            <KpiCard icon={CreditCard} label="Success Rate" value={summary ? `${summary.paymentSuccessRate}%` : "—"} trend={{ value: "+0.8%", up: true }} accent delay={0.2} />
            <KpiCard icon={TrendingUp} label="Conversion" value={summary ? `${summary.conversionRate}%` : "—"} trend={{ value: "-0.3%", up: false }} delay={0.25} />
          </>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Charts row */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 lg:grid-cols-2">
        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60 backdrop-blur">
          <CardHeader className="pb-2">
            <CardTitle className="text-sm">Revenue Trend (30 days)</CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent>
            {isLoading ? <Skeleton className="h-52 w-full" /> : (
              <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={208}>
                <AreaChart data={revenueData}>
                  <defs>
                    <linearGradient id="revGrad" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                      <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#3b82f6" stopOpacity={0.4} />
                      <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#3b82f6" stopOpacity={0} />
                    </linearGradient>
                  </defs>
                  <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#ffffff08" />
                  <XAxis dataKey="date" tickFormatter={fmtDate} tick={{ fill: "#64748b", fontSize: 10 }} />
                  <YAxis tick={{ fill: "#64748b", fontSize: 10 }} tickFormatter={(v: number) => `$${v}`} />
                  <Tooltip content={<ChartTip />} />
                  <Area type="monotone" dataKey="revenue" name="Revenue" stroke="#3b82f6" strokeWidth={2} fill="url(#revGrad)" />
                </AreaChart>
              </ResponsiveContainer>
            )}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60 backdrop-blur">
          <CardHeader className="pb-2">
            <CardTitle className="text-sm">Traffic Sources</CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent>
            {isLoading ? <Skeleton className="h-52 w-full" /> : (
              <>
                <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={180}>
                  <PieChart>
                    <Pie data={trafficData} dataKey="value" nameKey="source" cx="50%" cy="50%" innerRadius={50} outerRadius={80} paddingAngle={3}>
                      {trafficData.map((_, i) => <Cell key={i} fill={CHART_COLORS[i % CHART_COLORS.length]} />)}
                    </Pie>
                    <Tooltip content={<ChartTip />} />
                  </PieChart>
                </ResponsiveContainer>
                <div className="mt-1 flex flex-wrap justify-center gap-3">
                  {trafficData.map((t, i) => (
                    <div key={t.source} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs">
                      <span className="size-2 rounded-full" style={{ backgroundColor: CHART_COLORS[i % CHART_COLORS.length] }} />
                      <span className="text-muted-foreground">{t.source}</span>
                      <span className="font-medium">{t.value}%</span>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </>
            )}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      </div>

      {/* System / Quick Actions / Notifications */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 lg:grid-cols-3">
        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60 backdrop-blur">
          <CardHeader className="pb-2"><CardTitle className="text-sm">System Status</CardTitle></CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-2">
            {[
              { label: "Server", icon: Server },
              { label: "CDN", icon: Globe },
              { label: "Payments", icon: CreditCard },
              { label: "Database", icon: Activity },
            ].map((s) => (
              <div key={s.label} className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-muted-foreground">
                  <s.icon className="size-3.5" /> {s.label}
                </div>
                <Badge className="bg-green-500/10 text-green-400 border-green-500/20 text-[10px]">
                  <span className="mr-1 size-1.5 rounded-full bg-green-400" /> Operational
                </Badge>
              </div>
            ))}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60 backdrop-blur">
          <CardHeader className="pb-2"><CardTitle className="text-sm">Quick Actions</CardTitle></CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
            {[
              { label: "Add Product", icon: Package },
              { label: "Create Coupon", icon: Zap },
              { label: "Newsletter", icon: Bell },
              { label: "View Reports", icon: TrendingUp },
            ].map((a) => (
              <Button
                key={a.label}
                variant="outline"
                className="h-auto flex-col gap-1.5 border-white/10 bg-white/5 py-3 text-xs hover:bg-white/10"
                onClick={() => toast.message(`${a.label} — use the sidebar to navigate`)}
              >
                <a.icon className="size-4 text-primary" />
                {a.label}
              </Button>
            ))}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60 backdrop-blur">
          <CardHeader className="pb-2"><CardTitle className="text-sm">Recent Notifications</CardTitle></CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-2">
            {notifications.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="py-4 text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground">No activity</p>
            ) : (
              notifications.map((n) => (
                <div key={n._id} className="flex items-start gap-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 p-2 text-xs">
                  <div className="mt-0.5 size-1.5 shrink-0 rounded-full bg-primary" />
                  <div>
                    <p className="font-medium">{n.title}</p>
                    <p className="text-muted-foreground">{n.message}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))
            )}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      </div>

      {/* Recent orders + top products */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 lg:grid-cols-2">
        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60 backdrop-blur">
          <CardHeader className="pb-2"><CardTitle className="text-sm">Recent Orders</CardTitle></CardHeader>
          <CardContent>
            {recentOrders.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="py-6 text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground">No orders yet — load demo data</p>
            ) : (
              <div className="space-y-2">
                {recentOrders.map((o) => (
                  <div key={o._id} className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg bg-white/5 p-2.5">
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-sm font-semibold">{o.orderNumber}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{o.customerName} · {o.items.length} item(s)</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      <span className="text-sm font-bold">{fmt(o.total)}</span>
                      <Badge className={cn("text-[10px]", statusColor[o.status] ?? "bg-gray-500/15")}>{o.status}</Badge>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60 backdrop-blur">
          <CardHeader className="pb-2"><CardTitle className="text-sm">Top Products by Revenue</CardTitle></CardHeader>
          <CardContent>
            {topProducts.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="py-6 text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground">No product data yet</p>
            ) : (
              <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={220}>
                <BarChart data={topProducts} layout="vertical">
                  <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#ffffff08" />
                  <XAxis type="number" tick={{ fill: "#64748b", fontSize: 10 }} tickFormatter={(v: number) => `$${v}`} />
                  <YAxis type="category" dataKey="title" width={90} tick={{ fill: "#64748b", fontSize: 9 }} tickFormatter={(v: string) => v.length > 12 ? v.slice(0, 12) + "…" : v} />
                  <Tooltip content={<ChartTip />} cursor={{ fill: "#ffffff05" }} />
                  <Bar dataKey="revenue" name="Revenue" radius={[0, 4, 4, 0]}>
                    {topProducts.map((_, i) => <Cell key={i} fill={CHART_COLORS[i % CHART_COLORS.length]} />)}
                  </Bar>
                </BarChart>
              </ResponsiveContainer>
            )}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
}
import * as React from "react";
import { useQuery, useMutation } from "convex/react";
import { api } from "@/convex/_generated/api.js";
import { Search, MoreHorizontal, CheckCircle2, XCircle, Ban, UserCheck, Building2, Shield, UserPlus, RefreshCw } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card.tsx";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input.tsx";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button.tsx";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge.tsx";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton.tsx";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select.tsx";
import { DropdownMenu, DropdownMenuContent, DropdownMenuItem, DropdownMenuTrigger } from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu.tsx";
import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table.tsx";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils.ts";

const ROLE_BADGE: Record<string, string> = {
  ADMIN: "bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-400 border-rose-500/20",
  VENDOR: "bg-amber-400/15 text-amber-300 border-amber-400/20",
  CUSTOMER: "bg-blue-500/15 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/20",
  AFFILIATE: "bg-cyan-500/15 text-cyan-300 border-cyan-500/20",
};

export function AdminUsers() {
  const [search, setSearch] = React.useState("");
  const [role, setRole] = React.useState("ALL");
  const data = useQuery(api.users.listAdmin, { search: search || undefined, role: role !== "ALL" ? role : undefined });
  const verify = useMutation(api.users.verify);
  const ban = useMutation(api.users.ban);
  const updateRole = useMutation(api.users.updateRole);
  const stats = useQuery(api.users.stats);

  const users = data?.items ?? [];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Users</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Manage platform users, roles, and permissions</p>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Stats */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 sm:grid-cols-4">
        {[
          { label: "Total Users", value: stats?.total ?? "—" },
          { label: "Customers", value: stats?.customers ?? "—" },
          { label: "Vendors", value: stats?.vendors ?? "—" },
          { label: "Verified", value: stats?.verified ?? "—" },
        ].map((s) => (
          <Card key={s.label} className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">{s.label}</p>
              <p className="mt-1 text-xl font-bold">{s.value}</p>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Filters */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardContent className="flex flex-col gap-3 p-4 sm:flex-row sm:items-center">
          <div className="relative flex-1">
            <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 size-3.5 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground" />
            <Input value={search} onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder="Search by name or email..." className="h-8 border-white/10 bg-white/5 pl-8 text-sm" />
          </div>
          <Select value={role} onValueChange={setRole}>
            <SelectTrigger className="h-8 w-36 border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-sm">
              <SelectValue />
            </SelectTrigger>
            <SelectContent>
              <SelectItem value="ALL">All roles</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="CUSTOMER">Customer</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="VENDOR">Vendor</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="ADMIN">Admin</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="AFFILIATE">Affiliate</SelectItem>
            </SelectContent>
          </Select>
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{users.length} users</span>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* Table */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardContent className="p-0">
          {data === undefined ? (
            <div className="space-y-2 p-4">
              {Array.from({ length: 5 }).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-12 w-full" />)}
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
              <Table>
                <TableHeader>
                  <TableRow className="border-white/8 hover:bg-transparent">
                    <TableHead>User</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Role</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Verified</TableHead>
                    <TableHead className="text-right">Orders</TableHead>
                    <TableHead className="text-right">Reviews</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Vendor / Affiliate</TableHead>
                    <TableHead className="text-right">Actions</TableHead>
                  </TableRow>
                </TableHeader>
                <TableBody>
                  {users.map((u) => (
                    <TableRow key={u.id} className="border-white/8 hover:bg-white/3">
                      <TableCell>
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <span className="grid size-7 place-items-center rounded-full bg-primary/15 text-xs font-bold text-primary">
                            {u.name.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
                          </span>
                          <div>
                            <div className="text-sm font-medium">{u.name}</div>
                            <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{u.email}</div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell>
                        <Badge className={cn("text-[10px]", ROLE_BADGE[u.role] ?? "bg-muted text-muted-foreground")}>
                          {u.role.toLowerCase()}
                        </Badge>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell>
                        {u.verified ? <CheckCircle2 className="size-4 text-green-400" /> : <XCircle className="size-4 text-muted-foreground" />}
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-right tabular-nums text-sm">{u.orderCount}</TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-right tabular-nums text-sm">{u.reviewCount}</TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-xs">
                        {u.vendor ? (
                          <div>
                            <div className="font-medium">{u.vendor.storeName}</div>
                            <div className="text-muted-foreground">${u.vendor.totalRevenue.toLocaleString()} rev</div>
                          </div>
                        ) : u.affiliate ? (
                          <div>
                            <div className="font-mono font-medium">{u.affiliate.code}</div>
                            <div className="text-muted-foreground">${u.affiliate.earnings.toLocaleString()} earned</div>
                          </div>
                        ) : <span className="text-muted-foreground">—</span>}
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-right">
                        <DropdownMenu>
                          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
                            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="size-7">
                              <MoreHorizontal className="size-3.5" />
                            </Button>
                          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
                          <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="w-44 border-white/10 bg-card/95">
                            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => { verify({ id: u.id as Parameters<typeof verify>[0]["id"] }); toast.success(`${u.name} verified`); }}>
                              <UserCheck className="size-3.5" /> Verify user
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => { updateRole({ id: u.id as Parameters<typeof updateRole>[0]["id"], role: "VENDOR" }); toast.success(`${u.name} promoted to vendor`); }}>
                              <Building2 className="size-3.5" /> Make vendor
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => { updateRole({ id: u.id as Parameters<typeof updateRole>[0]["id"], role: "ADMIN" }); toast.success(`${u.name} promoted to admin`); }}>
                              <Shield className="size-3.5" /> Make admin
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                            <DropdownMenuItem className="text-destructive focus:text-destructive" onClick={() => { ban({ id: u.id as Parameters<typeof ban>[0]["id"] }); toast.success(`${u.name} banned`); }}>
                              <Ban className="size-3.5" /> Ban user
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                          </DropdownMenuContent>
                        </DropdownMenu>
                      </TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                  ))}
                  {users.length === 0 && (
                    <TableRow>
                      <TableCell colSpan={7} className="py-8 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                        No users match your filters. Load demo data first.
                      </TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                  )}
                </TableBody>
              </Table>
            </div>
          )}
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}
import * as React from "react";
import { useQuery, useMutation } from "convex/react";
import { api } from "@/convex/_generated/api.js";
import { Search, Plus, CheckCircle2, XCircle, MoreHorizontal, Star, Package } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card.tsx";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input.tsx";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button.tsx";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge.tsx";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton.tsx";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select.tsx";
import { DropdownMenu, DropdownMenuContent, DropdownMenuItem, DropdownMenuTrigger, DropdownMenuSeparator } from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu.tsx";
import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table.tsx";
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle, DialogTrigger } from "@/components/ui/dialog.tsx";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label.tsx";
import { Switch } from "@/components/ui/switch.tsx";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils.ts";

const STATUS_BADGE: Record<string, string> = {
  ACTIVE: "bg-green-500/15 text-green-400 border-green-500/20",
  DRAFT: "bg-gray-500/15 text-gray-400 border-gray-500/20",
  PENDING: "bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-400 border-amber-500/20",
  REJECTED: "bg-red-500/15 text-red-400 border-red-500/20",
};

export function AdminProducts() {
  const [search, setSearch] = React.useState("");
  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = React.useState("ALL");
  const [typeFilter, setTypeFilter] = React.useState("ALL");
  const [addOpen, setAddOpen] = React.useState(false);

  const data = useQuery(api.products.list, {
    status: statusFilter !== "ALL" ? statusFilter : undefined,
    type: typeFilter !== "ALL" ? typeFilter : undefined,
    search: search || undefined,
  });
  const pendingData = useQuery(api.products.pending);
  const approve = useMutation(api.products.approve);
  const reject = useMutation(api.products.reject);
  const updateProduct = useMutation(api.products.update);
  const removeProduct = useMutation(api.products.remove);
  const createProduct = useMutation(api.products.create);

  const products = data?.items ?? [];
  const pending = pendingData?.items ?? [];

  // New product form
  const [newTitle, setNewTitle] = React.useState("");
  const [newType, setNewType] = React.useState("TEMPLATE");
  const [newPrice, setNewPrice] = React.useState("");
  const [newStatus, setNewStatus] = React.useState("ACTIVE");
  const [newFeatured, setNewFeatured] = React.useState(false);
  const [saving, setSaving] = React.useState(false);

  const handleCreate = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!newTitle || !newPrice) return;
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      await createProduct({ title: newTitle, type: newType, price: Number(newPrice), status: newStatus, featured: newFeatured, tags: [] });
      toast.success("Product created");
      setAddOpen(false);
      setNewTitle(""); setNewPrice("");
    } catch { toast.error("Failed to create product"); }
    finally { setSaving(false); }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Products</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Manage your digital product catalog</p>
        </div>
        <Dialog open={addOpen} onOpenChange={setAddOpen}>
          <DialogTrigger asChild>
            <Button size="sm" className="gap-1.5 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent hover:opacity-90">
              <Plus className="size-3.5" /> Add Product
            </Button>
          </DialogTrigger>
          <DialogContent className="border-white/10 bg-card">
            <DialogHeader>
              <DialogTitle>Add New Product</DialogTitle>
            </DialogHeader>
            <form onSubmit={handleCreate} className="space-y-4">
              <div className="space-y-1.5">
                <Label className="text-xs">Title</Label>
                <Input value={newTitle} onChange={(e) => setNewTitle(e.target.value)} placeholder="Product name" className="border-white/10 bg-white/5" required />
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                <div className="space-y-1.5">
                  <Label className="text-xs">Type</Label>
                  <Select value={newType} onValueChange={setNewType}>
                    <SelectTrigger className="border-white/10 bg-white/5"><SelectValue /></SelectTrigger>
                    <SelectContent>
                      {["TEMPLATE", "PLUGIN", "AI_TOOL", "GAME", "GIFT_CARD", "IPTV", "OTHER"].map((t) => (
                        <SelectItem key={t} value={t}>{t.replace(/_/g, " ")}</SelectItem>
                      ))}
                    </SelectContent>
                  </Select>
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-1.5">
                  <Label className="text-xs">Price (USD)</Label>
                  <Input type="number" value={newPrice} onChange={(e) => setNewPrice(e.target.value)} placeholder="49" className="border-white/10 bg-white/5" required />
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-3">
                <span className="text-sm">Featured product</span>
                <Switch checked={newFeatured} onCheckedChange={setNewFeatured} />
              </div>
              <Button type="submit" disabled={saving} className="w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent hover:opacity-90">
                {saving ? "Creating..." : "Create Product"}
              </Button>
            </form>
          </DialogContent>
        </Dialog>
      </div>

      {/* Pending approvals */}
      {pending.length > 0 && (
        <Card className="border-amber-500/20 bg-amber-500/5">
          <CardHeader className="pb-2">
            <CardTitle className="text-sm text-amber-400">{pending.length} products awaiting approval</CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-2">
            {pending.map((p) => (
              <div key={p._id} className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border border-white/8 bg-white/5 p-3">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">{p.title}</p>
                  <Badge variant="outline" className="mt-1 border-white/10 text-[10px]">{p.type}</Badge>
                </div>
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  <Button size="sm" variant="outline" className="h-7 border-destructive/30 text-destructive hover:bg-destructive/10"
                    onClick={() => { reject({ id: p._id }); toast.success("Rejected"); }}>
                    <XCircle className="size-3.5" /> Reject
                  </Button>
                  <Button size="sm" className="h-7 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700"
                    onClick={() => { approve({ id: p._id }); toast.success("Approved & published"); }}>
                    <CheckCircle2 className="size-3.5" /> Approve
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      )}

      {/* Filters */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardContent className="flex flex-col gap-3 p-4 sm:flex-row sm:items-center">
          <div className="relative flex-1">
            <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 size-3.5 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground" />
            <Input value={search} onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder="Search products..." className="h-8 border-white/10 bg-white/5 pl-8 text-sm" />
          </div>
          <Select value={statusFilter} onValueChange={setStatusFilter}>
            <SelectTrigger className="h-8 w-32 border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-sm"><SelectValue /></SelectTrigger>
            <SelectContent>
              <SelectItem value="ALL">All status</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="ACTIVE">Active</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="DRAFT">Draft</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="PENDING">Pending</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="REJECTED">Rejected</SelectItem>
            </SelectContent>
          </Select>
          <Select value={typeFilter} onValueChange={setTypeFilter}>
            <SelectTrigger className="h-8 w-32 border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-sm"><SelectValue /></SelectTrigger>
            <SelectContent>
              <SelectItem value="ALL">All types</SelectItem>
              {["TEMPLATE", "PLUGIN", "AI_TOOL", "GAME", "GIFT_CARD", "IPTV"].map((t) => (
                <SelectItem key={t} value={t}>{t.replace(/_/g, " ")}</SelectItem>
              ))}
            </SelectContent>
          </Select>
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{products.length} products</span>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* Table */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardContent className="p-0">
          {data === undefined ? (
            <div className="space-y-2 p-4">{Array.from({ length: 5 }).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-12 w-full" />)}</div>
          ) : (
            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
              <Table>
                <TableHeader>
                  <TableRow className="border-white/8 hover:bg-transparent">
                    <TableHead>Product</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Type</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Status</TableHead>
                    <TableHead className="text-right">Price</TableHead>
                    <TableHead className="text-right">Sales</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Rating</TableHead>
                    <TableHead className="text-right">Actions</TableHead>
                  </TableRow>
                </TableHeader>
                <TableBody>
                  {products.map((p) => (
                    <TableRow key={p._id} className="border-white/8 hover:bg-white/3">
                      <TableCell>
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <div className="grid size-7 place-items-center rounded-lg bg-primary/10">
                            <Package className="size-3.5 text-primary" />
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <div className="text-sm font-medium line-clamp-1">{p.title}</div>
                            <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{p.sku}</div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell>
                        <Badge variant="outline" className="border-white/10 text-[10px]">{p.type.replace(/_/g, " ")}</Badge>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell>
                        <Badge className={cn("text-[10px]", STATUS_BADGE[p.status] ?? "bg-muted")}>{p.status}</Badge>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-right tabular-nums text-sm">
                        <span className="font-semibold">${p.effectivePrice}</span>
                        {p.discountPercent > 0 && <span className="ml-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground line-through">${p.price}</span>}
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-right tabular-nums text-sm">{p.salesCount.toLocaleString()}</TableCell>
                      <TableCell>
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                          <Star className="size-3 fill-amber-400 text-amber-400" />
                          <span className="text-xs">{p.rating.toFixed(1)}</span>
                        </div>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-right">
                        <DropdownMenu>
                          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
                            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="size-7"><MoreHorizontal className="size-3.5" /></Button>
                          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
                          <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="border-white/10 bg-card/95">
                            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => { updateProduct({ id: p._id, featured: !p.featured }); toast.success(p.featured ? "Unfeatured" : "Featured"); }}>
                              <Star className="size-3.5" /> {p.featured ? "Unfeature" : "Feature"}
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => { updateProduct({ id: p._id, status: p.status === "ACTIVE" ? "DRAFT" : "ACTIVE" }); toast.success("Status updated"); }}>
                              {p.status === "ACTIVE" ? <><XCircle className="size-3.5" /> Unpublish</> : <><CheckCircle2 className="size-3.5" /> Publish</>}
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                            <DropdownMenuSeparator className="bg-white/8" />
                            <DropdownMenuItem className="text-destructive focus:text-destructive" onClick={() => { removeProduct({ id: p._id }); toast.success("Product deleted"); }}>
                              <XCircle className="size-3.5" /> Delete
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                          </DropdownMenuContent>
                        </DropdownMenu>
                      </TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                  ))}
                  {products.length === 0 && (
                    <TableRow><TableCell colSpan={7} className="py-8 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">No products found. Load demo data to get started.</TableCell></TableRow>
                  )}
                </TableBody>
              </Table>
            </div>
          )}
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}
import * as React from "react";
import { useQuery, useMutation } from "convex/react";
import { api } from "@/convex/_generated/api.js";
import { Search, MoreHorizontal, RefreshCw, DollarSign, ShoppingCart, Clock, XCircle } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card.tsx";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input.tsx";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button.tsx";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge.tsx";
import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton.tsx";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select.tsx";
import { DropdownMenu, DropdownMenuContent, DropdownMenuItem, DropdownMenuTrigger } from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu.tsx";
import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table.tsx";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils.ts";

const STATUS_BADGE: Record<string, string> = {
  COMPLETED: "bg-green-500/15 text-green-400 border-green-500/20",
  PAID: "bg-blue-500/15 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/20",
  PENDING: "bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-400 border-amber-500/20",
  REFUNDED: "bg-red-500/15 text-red-400 border-red-500/20",
  CANCELLED: "bg-gray-500/15 text-gray-400 border-gray-500/20",
};

function fmtDate(ts: number) {
  return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("en-US", { month: "short", day: "numeric", year: "numeric" }).format(new Date(ts));
}

export function AdminOrders() {
  const [search, setSearch] = React.useState("");
  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = React.useState("ALL");
  const data = useQuery(api.orders.list, { status: statusFilter !== "ALL" ? statusFilter : undefined, search: search || undefined });
  const stats = useQuery(api.orders.stats);
  const updateStatus = useMutation(api.orders.updateStatus);
  const refund = useMutation(api.orders.refund);

  const orders = data?.items ?? [];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Orders</h1>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">View and manage customer orders</p>
      </div>

      {/* Stats */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 sm:grid-cols-4">
        {[
          { label: "Total Orders", value: stats?.total ?? "—", icon: ShoppingCart },
          { label: "Completed", value: stats?.completed ?? "—", icon: RefreshCw },
          { label: "Pending", value: stats?.pending ?? "—", icon: Clock },
          { label: "Revenue", value: stats ? `$${(stats.revenue).toLocaleString()}` : "—", icon: DollarSign },
        ].map((s) => (
          <Card key={s.label} className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
            <CardContent className="flex items-center gap-3 p-4">
              <div className="grid size-8 place-items-center rounded-lg bg-primary/10">
                <s.icon className="size-4 text-primary" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">{s.label}</p>
                <p className="text-lg font-bold">{s.value}</p>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Filters */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardContent className="flex flex-col gap-3 p-4 sm:flex-row sm:items-center">
          <div className="relative flex-1">
            <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 size-3.5 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground" />
            <Input value={search} onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder="Search by order # or customer..." className="h-8 border-white/10 bg-white/5 pl-8 text-sm" />
          </div>
          <Select value={statusFilter} onValueChange={setStatusFilter}>
            <SelectTrigger className="h-8 w-36 border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-sm"><SelectValue /></SelectTrigger>
            <SelectContent>
              <SelectItem value="ALL">All status</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="COMPLETED">Completed</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="PAID">Paid</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="PENDING">Pending</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="REFUNDED">Refunded</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="CANCELLED">Cancelled</SelectItem>
            </SelectContent>
          </Select>
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{orders.length} orders</span>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* Table */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardContent className="p-0">
          {data === undefined ? (
            <div className="space-y-2 p-4">{Array.from({ length: 6 }).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-12 w-full" />)}</div>
          ) : (
            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
              <Table>
                <TableHeader>
                  <TableRow className="border-white/8 hover:bg-transparent">
                    <TableHead>Order</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Customer</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Status</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Provider</TableHead>
                    <TableHead className="text-right">Total</TableHead>
                    <TableHead>Date</TableHead>
                    <TableHead className="text-right">Actions</TableHead>
                  </TableRow>
                </TableHeader>
                <TableBody>
                  {orders.map((o) => (
                    <TableRow key={o._id} className="border-white/8 hover:bg-white/3">
                      <TableCell>
                        <div className="text-sm font-mono font-semibold">{o.orderNumber}</div>
                        <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{o.items.length} item(s)</div>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell>
                        <div className="text-sm font-medium">{o.customerName}</div>
                        <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{o.customerEmail}</div>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell>
                        <Badge className={cn("text-[10px]", STATUS_BADGE[o.status] ?? "bg-muted")}>{o.status}</Badge>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell>
                        <Badge variant="outline" className="border-white/10 text-[10px]">{o.provider ?? "—"}</Badge>
                      </TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-right font-semibold tabular-nums">${o.total.toFixed(2)}</TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{fmtDate(o._creationTime)}</TableCell>
                      <TableCell className="text-right">
                        <DropdownMenu>
                          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
                            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="size-7"><MoreHorizontal className="size-3.5" /></Button>
                          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
                          <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="border-white/10 bg-card/95">
                            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => { updateStatus({ id: o._id, status: "COMPLETED" }); toast.success("Order marked completed"); }}>
                              Mark completed
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => { updateStatus({ id: o._id, status: "PENDING" }); toast.success("Order set to pending"); }}>
                              Set pending
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                            <DropdownMenuItem className="text-destructive focus:text-destructive" onClick={() => { refund({ id: o._id }); toast.success("Refund processed"); }}>
                              <XCircle className="size-3.5" /> Refund
                            </DropdownMenuItem>
                          </DropdownMenuContent>
                        </DropdownMenu>
                      </TableCell>
                    </TableRow>
                  ))}
                  {orders.length === 0 && (
                    <TableRow><TableCell colSpan={7} className="py-8 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">No orders found. Load demo data first.</TableCell></TableRow>
                  )}
                </TableBody>
              </Table>
            </div>
          )}
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}
import * as React from "react";
import { useQuery, useMutation } from "convex/react";
import { api } from "@/convex/_generated/api.js";
import { Plus, Ticket, CheckCircle2, XCircle, Pencil, Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card.tsx";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input.tsx";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button.tsx";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge.tsx";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label.tsx";
import { Switch } from "@/components/ui/switch.tsx";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select.tsx";
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle, DialogTrigger } from "@/components/ui/dialog.tsx";
import { Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow } from "@/components/ui/table.tsx";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils.ts";

export function AdminCoupons() {
  const data = useQuery(api.coupons.list);
  const createCoupon = useMutation(api.coupons.create);
  const toggleCoupon = useMutation(api.coupons.toggle);
  const removeCoupon = useMutation(api.coupons.remove);

  const [addOpen, setAddOpen] = React.useState(false);
  const [code, setCode] = React.useState("");
  const [type, setType] = React.useState("PERCENTAGE");
  const [value, setValue] = React.useState("");
  const [minPurchase, setMinPurchase] = React.useState("0");
  const [usageLimit, setUsageLimit] = React.useState("");
  const [saving, setSaving] = React.useState(false);

  const coupons = data?.items ?? [];
  const active = coupons.filter((c) => c.active).length;

  const handleCreate = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      await createCoupon({
        code: code.toUpperCase(),
        type,
        value: Number(value),
        minPurchase: Number(minPurchase),
        active: true,
        usageLimit: usageLimit ? Number(usageLimit) : undefined,
      });
      toast.success("Coupon created");
      setAddOpen(false);
      setCode(""); setValue(""); setMinPurchase("0"); setUsageLimit("");
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to create coupon");
    } finally { setSaving(false); }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Coupons</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Create and manage discount codes</p>
        </div>
        <Dialog open={addOpen} onOpenChange={setAddOpen}>
          <DialogTrigger asChild>
            <Button size="sm" className="gap-1.5 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent hover:opacity-90">
              <Plus className="size-3.5" /> New Coupon
            </Button>
          </DialogTrigger>
          <DialogContent className="border-white/10 bg-card">
            <DialogHeader><DialogTitle>Create Coupon</DialogTitle></DialogHeader>
            <form onSubmit={handleCreate} className="space-y-4">
              <div className="space-y-1.5">
                <Label className="text-xs">Coupon Code</Label>
                <Input value={code} onChange={(e) => setCode(e.target.value.toUpperCase())} placeholder="SAVE20" className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 font-mono uppercase" required />
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                <div className="space-y-1.5">
                  <Label className="text-xs">Type</Label>
                  <Select value={type} onValueChange={setType}>
                    <SelectTrigger className="border-white/10 bg-white/5"><SelectValue /></SelectTrigger>
                    <SelectContent>
                      <SelectItem value="PERCENTAGE">Percentage (%)</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="FIXED">Fixed Amount ($)</SelectItem>
                    </SelectContent>
                  </Select>
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-1.5">
                  <Label className="text-xs">Value</Label>
                  <Input type="number" value={value} onChange={(e) => setValue(e.target.value)} placeholder={type === "PERCENTAGE" ? "20" : "10"} className="border-white/10 bg-white/5" required />
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                <div className="space-y-1.5">
                  <Label className="text-xs">Min Purchase ($)</Label>
                  <Input type="number" value={minPurchase} onChange={(e) => setMinPurchase(e.target.value)} placeholder="0" className="border-white/10 bg-white/5" />
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-1.5">
                  <Label className="text-xs">Usage Limit</Label>
                  <Input type="number" value={usageLimit} onChange={(e) => setUsageLimit(e.target.value)} placeholder="Unlimited" className="border-white/10 bg-white/5" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <Button type="submit" disabled={saving} className="w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent hover:opacity-90">
                {saving ? "Creating..." : "Create Coupon"}
              </Button>
            </form>
          </DialogContent>
        </Dialog>
      </div>

      {/* Stats */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
        {[
          { label: "Total Coupons", value: coupons.length },
          { label: "Active", value: active },
          { label: "Inactive", value: coupons.length - active },
        ].map((s) => (
          <Card key={s.label} className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">{s.label}</p>
              <p className="mt-1 text-xl font-bold">{s.value}</p>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Coupon table */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardContent className="p-0">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <Table>
              <TableHeader>
                <TableRow className="border-white/8 hover:bg-transparent">
                  <TableHead>Code</TableHead>
                  <TableHead>Type</TableHead>
                  <TableHead>Discount</TableHead>
                  <TableHead>Min Purchase</TableHead>
                  <TableHead>Usage</TableHead>
                  <TableHead>Status</TableHead>
                  <TableHead className="text-right">Actions</TableHead>
                </TableRow>
              </TableHeader>
              <TableBody>
                {coupons.map((c) => (
                  <TableRow key={c._id} className="border-white/8 hover:bg-white/3">
                    <TableCell>
                      <span className="font-mono text-sm font-semibold text-primary">{c.code}</span>
                    </TableCell>
                    <TableCell>
                      <Badge variant="outline" className="border-white/10 text-[10px]">{c.type}</Badge>
                    </TableCell>
                    <TableCell className="text-sm font-semibold">
                      {c.type === "PERCENTAGE" ? `${c.value}%` : `$${c.value}`}
                    </TableCell>
                    <TableCell className="text-sm">{c.minPurchase > 0 ? `$${c.minPurchase}` : "None"}</TableCell>
                    <TableCell className="text-sm">
                      {c.usageCount} {c.usageLimit ? `/ ${c.usageLimit}` : ""}
                    </TableCell>
                    <TableCell>
                      <Switch
                        checked={c.active}
                        onCheckedChange={(active) => {
                          toggleCoupon({ id: c._id, active });
                          toast.success(active ? "Coupon activated" : "Coupon deactivated");
                        }}
                      />
                    </TableCell>
                    <TableCell className="text-right">
                      <Button
                        variant="ghost"
                        size="icon"
                        className="size-7 text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive"
                        onClick={() => { removeCoupon({ id: c._id }); toast.success("Coupon deleted"); }}
                      >
                        <Trash2 className="size-3.5" />
                      </Button>
                    </TableCell>
                  </TableRow>
                ))}
                {coupons.length === 0 && (
                  <TableRow>
                    <TableCell colSpan={7} className="py-8 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                      <Ticket className="mx-auto mb-2 size-8 text-muted-foreground/30" />
                      No coupons yet. Create your first discount code.
                    </TableCell>
                  </TableRow>
                )}
              </TableBody>
            </Table>
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}
import * as React from "react";
import { useQuery, useMutation } from "convex/react";
import { api } from "@/convex/_generated/api.js";
import { Save, Loader2, CreditCard, Settings, Globe, Palette } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card.tsx";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input.tsx";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button.tsx";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label.tsx";
import { Switch } from "@/components/ui/switch.tsx";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select.tsx";
import { Slider } from "@/components/ui/slider.tsx";
import { toast } from "sonner";

export function AdminSettings() {
  const data = useQuery(api.settings.list);
  const setSettings = useMutation(api.settings.setBatch);

  const cfg = data?.settings ?? {};

  const [siteName, setSiteName] = React.useState("");
  const [currency, setCurrency] = React.useState("USD");
  const [commission, setCommission] = React.useState(15);
  const [maintenance, setMaintenance] = React.useState(false);
  const [gateways, setGateways] = React.useState({ stripe: true, paypal: true, jazzcash: true, lemon_squeezy: true });
  const [saving, setSaving] = React.useState(false);
  const [initialized, setInitialized] = React.useState(false);

  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!data || initialized) return;
    setSiteName(cfg["site_name"] ?? "PlayBeat Digital");
    setCurrency(cfg["currency"] ?? "USD");
    setCommission(Number(cfg["commission_rate"] ?? 15));
    setMaintenance(cfg["maintenance_mode"] === "true");
    setGateways({
      stripe: cfg["stripe_active"] !== "false",
      paypal: cfg["paypal_active"] !== "false",
      jazzcash: cfg["jazzcash_active"] !== "false",
      lemon_squeezy: cfg["lemon_squeezy_active"] !== "false",
    });
    setInitialized(true);
  }, [data, initialized, cfg]);

  const save = async () => {
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      await setSettings({
        settings: [
          { key: "site_name", value: siteName, category: "general" },
          { key: "currency", value: currency, category: "general" },
          { key: "commission_rate", value: String(commission), category: "commerce" },
          { key: "maintenance_mode", value: String(maintenance), category: "system" },
          { key: "stripe_active", value: String(gateways.stripe), category: "payments" },
          { key: "paypal_active", value: String(gateways.paypal), category: "payments" },
          { key: "jazzcash_active", value: String(gateways.jazzcash), category: "payments" },
          { key: "lemon_squeezy_active", value: String(gateways.lemon_squeezy), category: "payments" },
        ],
      });
      toast.success("Settings saved");
    } catch { toast.error("Failed to save settings"); }
    finally { setSaving(false); }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Settings</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Configure your PlayBeat platform</p>
        </div>
        <Button onClick={save} disabled={saving} className="gap-1.5 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent hover:opacity-90">
          {saving ? <Loader2 className="size-4 animate-spin" /> : <Save className="size-4" />}
          Save Settings
        </Button>
      </div>

      <div className="grid gap-4 lg:grid-cols-2">
        {/* General Settings */}
        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
          <CardHeader className="pb-3">
            <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <Settings className="size-4 text-primary" /> General
            </CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-4">
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Site Name</Label>
              <Input value={siteName} onChange={(e) => setSiteName(e.target.value)} className="border-white/10 bg-white/5" />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Display Currency</Label>
              <Select value={currency} onValueChange={setCurrency}>
                <SelectTrigger className="border-white/10 bg-white/5"><SelectValue /></SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  <SelectItem value="USD">USD — US Dollar</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="PKR">PKR — Pakistani Rupee</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="EUR">EUR — Euro</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="GBP">GBP — British Pound</SelectItem>
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                <Label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Default Commission Rate</Label>
                <span className="text-sm font-bold text-primary">{commission}%</span>
              </div>
              <Slider value={[commission]} onValueChange={(v) => setCommission(v[0])} min={5} max={40} step={1} className="py-1" />
              <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
                <span>5%</span><span>40%</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-3">
              <div>
                <p className="text-sm font-medium">Maintenance Mode</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Disable checkout for all users</p>
              </div>
              <Switch checked={maintenance} onCheckedChange={setMaintenance} />
            </div>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* Payment Gateways */}
        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
          <CardHeader className="pb-3">
            <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <CreditCard className="size-4 text-primary" /> Payment Gateways
            </CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-2">
            {(Object.entries(gateways) as Array<[keyof typeof gateways, boolean]>).map(([k, v]) => (
              <div key={k} className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <CreditCard className="size-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
                  <span className="text-sm font-medium capitalize">{k.replace(/_/g, " ")}</span>
                </div>
                <Switch checked={v} onCheckedChange={(c) => setGateways((g) => ({ ...g, [k]: c }))} />
              </div>
            ))}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* Store Appearance */}
        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
          <CardHeader className="pb-3">
            <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <Palette className="size-4 text-primary" /> Store Appearance
            </CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-3">
            {[
              { label: "Dark Mode", defaultOn: true },
              { label: "Show Vendor Badges", defaultOn: true },
              { label: "Show Reviews", defaultOn: true },
              { label: "Show Sale Banners", defaultOn: false },
            ].map((item) => (
              <div key={item.label} className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-3">
                <span className="text-sm">{item.label}</span>
                <Switch defaultChecked={item.defaultOn} onCheckedChange={() => toast.message("Appearance setting updated")} />
              </div>
            ))}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* Notifications */}
        <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
          <CardHeader className="pb-3">
            <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <Globe className="size-4 text-primary" /> Notifications
            </CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-3">
            {[
              { label: "Email on new order", defaultOn: true },
              { label: "Email on refund request", defaultOn: true },
              { label: "Email on new vendor signup", defaultOn: false },
              { label: "SMS on large orders ($500+)", defaultOn: false },
            ].map((item) => (
              <div key={item.label} className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-3">
                <span className="text-sm">{item.label}</span>
                <Switch defaultChecked={item.defaultOn} onCheckedChange={() => toast.message("Notification setting updated")} />
              </div>
            ))}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
import * as React from "react";
import { CreditCard, CheckCircle2, XCircle, ExternalLink, Zap, AlertTriangle } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card.tsx";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button.tsx";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge.tsx";
import { Switch } from "@/components/ui/switch.tsx";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input.tsx";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label.tsx";
import { toast } from "sonner";

const GATEWAYS = [
  { id: "stripe", name: "Stripe", desc: "Global payments via credit/debit cards", active: true, mode: "live", color: "#635bff", fees: "2.9% + 30¢" },
  { id: "paypal", name: "PayPal", desc: "PayPal and card payments worldwide", active: true, mode: "live", color: "#003087", fees: "3.49% + 49¢" },
  { id: "jazzcash", name: "JazzCash", desc: "Pakistan mobile wallet payments", active: true, mode: "sandbox", color: "#d5222a", fees: "1.5%" },
  { id: "lemon_squeezy", name: "Lemon Squeezy", desc: "Merchant of record for digital products", active: true, mode: "live", color: "#ffd700", fees: "5% + 50¢" },
  { id: "crypto", name: "Crypto (USDT/BTC)", desc: "Accept cryptocurrency payments", active: false, mode: "off", color: "#f7931a", fees: "0.5%" },
  { id: "bank", name: "Bank Transfer", desc: "Manual bank wire transfer", active: false, mode: "off", color: "#4caf50", fees: "Free" },
];

export function AdminPayments() {
  const [gateways, setGateways] = React.useState(GATEWAYS);

  const toggle = (id: string) => {
    setGateways((prev) => prev.map((g) => g.id === id ? { ...g, active: !g.active } : g));
    toast.success("Gateway updated");
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Payment Gateways</h1>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Configure and manage payment providers</p>
      </div>

      {/* Summary */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
        {[
          { label: "Total Gateways", value: gateways.length },
          { label: "Active", value: gateways.filter((g) => g.active).length },
          { label: "Live", value: gateways.filter((g) => g.mode === "live").length },
        ].map((s) => (
          <Card key={s.label} className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">{s.label}</p>
              <p className="mt-1 text-xl font-bold">{s.value}</p>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Gateway cards */}
      <div className="grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2">
        {gateways.map((g) => (
          <Card key={g.id} className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <div className="grid size-9 place-items-center rounded-lg" style={{ background: `${g.color}20` }}>
                    <CreditCard className="size-4" style={{ color: g.color }} />
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold">{g.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{g.desc}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <Switch checked={g.active} onCheckedChange={() => toggle(g.id)} />
              </div>
              <div className="mt-3 flex items-center gap-2">
                <Badge variant="outline" className="border-white/10 text-[10px]">Fees: {g.fees}</Badge>
                <Badge className={
                  g.mode === "live" ? "bg-green-500/15 text-green-400 border-green-500/20 text-[10px]" :
                  g.mode === "sandbox" ? "bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-400 border-amber-500/20 text-[10px]" :
                  "bg-gray-500/15 text-gray-400 text-[10px]"
                }>
                  {g.mode === "live" ? <><CheckCircle2 className="size-2.5" /> Live</> :
                   g.mode === "sandbox" ? <><AlertTriangle className="size-2.5" /> Sandbox</> :
                   <><XCircle className="size-2.5" /> Off</>}
                </Badge>
                {g.active && (
                  <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="ml-auto h-6 gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
                    onClick={() => toast.message(`Configure ${g.name} — add API keys in Secrets tab`)}>
                    <Zap className="size-3" /> Configure
                  </Button>
                )}
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* API Key section */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardHeader className="pb-3">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm">Stripe Configuration</CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent className="space-y-3">
          <div className="rounded-lg border border-amber-500/20 bg-amber-500/5 p-3 text-xs text-amber-400">
            API keys are stored securely in your Secrets tab. Never share or expose them.
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-1.5">
            <Label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Publishable Key</Label>
            <Input type="password" placeholder="pk_live_..." className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 font-mono text-xs" />
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-1.5">
            <Label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Secret Key</Label>
            <Input type="password" placeholder="sk_live_..." className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 font-mono text-xs" />
          </div>
          <Button className="gap-1.5 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-accent hover:opacity-90"
            onClick={() => toast.message("Store keys in the Secrets tab under Advanced settings")}>
            <ExternalLink className="size-3.5" /> Open Secrets Tab
          </Button>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}
import * as React from "react";
import { useQuery } from "convex/react";
import { api } from "@/convex/_generated/api.js";
import { Download, FileText, Calendar, TrendingUp, DollarSign } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card.tsx";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button.tsx";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select.tsx";
import { Area, AreaChart, ResponsiveContainer, Tooltip, XAxis, YAxis, CartesianGrid } from "recharts";
import { toast } from "sonner";

function ChartTip({ active, payload, label }: { active?: boolean; payload?: Array<{ name: string; value: number; color: string }>; label?: string }) {
  if (!active || !payload?.length) return null;
  return (
    <div className="rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-black/80 px-3 py-2 text-xs">
      <p className="mb-1 font-medium">{label}</p>
      {payload.map((p, i) => <p key={i} style={{ color: p.color }}>{p.name}: {p.value}</p>)}
    </div>
  );
}

export function AdminReports() {
  const [period, setPeriod] = React.useState("30");
  const dash = useQuery(api.analytics.dashboard);
  const orders = useQuery(api.orders.stats);

  const revenueData = (dash?.revenueTimeseries ?? []).slice(-Number(period));

  const monthly = revenueData.reduce((s, d) => s + d.revenue, 0);
  const avgDaily = revenueData.length > 0 ? monthly / revenueData.length : 0;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Reports</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Financial reports and business insights</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Select value={period} onValueChange={setPeriod}>
            <SelectTrigger className="h-8 w-32 border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-sm"><SelectValue /></SelectTrigger>
            <SelectContent>
              <SelectItem value="7">Last 7 days</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="14">Last 14 days</SelectItem>
              <SelectItem value="30">Last 30 days</SelectItem>
            </SelectContent>
          </Select>
          <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="gap-1.5 border-white/10 bg-white/5"
            onClick={() => toast.message("Export — CSV download would be generated here")}>
            <Download className="size-3.5" /> Export
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Summary cards */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 lg:grid-cols-4">
        {[
          { label: "Period Revenue", value: `$${monthly.toFixed(0)}`, icon: DollarSign, color: "text-primary" },
          { label: "Avg Daily Revenue", value: `$${avgDaily.toFixed(0)}`, icon: TrendingUp, color: "text-accent" },
          { label: "Total Orders", value: orders?.total ?? "—", icon: FileText, color: "text-green-400" },
          { label: "Refunds", value: orders?.refunded ?? "—", icon: Calendar, color: "text-red-400" },
        ].map((s) => (
          <Card key={s.label} className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
            <CardContent className="flex items-center gap-3 p-4">
              <div className="grid size-8 place-items-center rounded-lg bg-white/5">
                <s.icon className={`size-4 ${s.color}`} />
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">{s.label}</p>
                <p className="text-lg font-bold">{s.value}</p>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Revenue chart */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardHeader className="pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm">Revenue Over Time</CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={300}>
            <AreaChart data={revenueData}>
              <defs>
                <linearGradient id="repRevGrad" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                  <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#3b82f6" stopOpacity={0.4} />
                  <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#3b82f6" stopOpacity={0} />
                </linearGradient>
              </defs>
              <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#ffffff08" />
              <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fill: "#64748b", fontSize: 10 }} tickFormatter={(v: string) => v.slice(5)} />
              <YAxis tick={{ fill: "#64748b", fontSize: 10 }} tickFormatter={(v: number) => `$${v}`} />
              <Tooltip content={<ChartTip />} />
              <Area type="monotone" dataKey="revenue" name="Revenue" stroke="#3b82f6" strokeWidth={2} fill="url(#repRevGrad)" />
              <Area type="monotone" dataKey="orders" name="Orders" stroke="#8b5cf6" strokeWidth={1.5} fill="none" />
            </AreaChart>
          </ResponsiveContainer>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* Category revenue */}
      <Card className="border-white/8 bg-card/60">
        <CardHeader className="pb-2">
          <CardTitle className="text-sm">Revenue by Category</CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {(dash?.revenueByCategory ?? []).map((c) => {
              const total = (dash?.revenueByCategory ?? []).reduce((s, x) => s + x.revenue, 0);
              const pct = total > 0 ? Math.round((c.revenue / total) * 100) : 0;
              return (
                <div key={c.name} className="space-y-1">
